|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-903">数据市场 (data mart)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-903">data mart</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-904">数据仓库内容的子集，往往包含针对部门级别或针对特定业务领域的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-904">A subset of the contents of a data warehouse that tends to contain data focused at the department level, or on a specific business area.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-972">数据库管理器 (database manager)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-972">database manager</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-973">物理数据库和用户之间的软件层。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-973">A layer of software between the physical database and the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-974">该 DBMS 管理对数据库的所有访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-974">The DBMS manages all access to the database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-975">数据库镜像</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-975">database mirroring</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-976">将对读写数据库（主体数据库）所做的每次更新立即重新生成到驻留在单独的数据库引擎实例（镜像服务器）中的该数据库的只读镜像（镜像数据库）中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-976">Immediately reproducing every update to a read-write database (the principal database) onto a read-only mirror of that database (the mirror database) residing on a separate instance of the database engine (the mirror server).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-977">在生产环境中，该镜像服务器位于其他的计算机上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-977">In production environments, the mirror server is on another machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-978">通过还原（但不恢复）主体数据库的完整备份可创建镜像数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-978">The mirror database is created by restoring a full backup of the principal database (without recovery).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-979">数据库镜像监视器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-979">Database Mirroring Monitor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-980">用于监视某一服务器实例上镜像数据库的任何子集的工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-980">A tool used to monitor any subset of the mirrored databases on a server instance.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1023">DBMS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1023">DBMS</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1024">物理数据库和用户之间的软件层。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1024">A layer of software between the physical database and the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1025">该 DBMS 管理对数据库的所有访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1025">The DBMS manages all access to the database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1026">DDL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1026">DDL</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1027">定义数据库的所有特性和属性（特别是记录布局、字段定义、键字段、文件位置和存储策略）的一种语言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1027">A language that defines all attributes and properties of a database, especially record layouts, field definitions, key fields, file locations, and storage strategy.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1135">维度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1135">dimension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1136">将数据组织到多个层中的多维数据集的一种结构属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1136">A structural attribute of a cube that organizes data into levels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1137">例如，Geography 维度可以包含成员 Country、Region、State 或 Province 以及 City。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1137">For example, a Geography dimension might include the members Country, Region, State or Province, and City.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1143">维度层次结构 (dimension hierarchy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1143">dimension hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1144">一种按每个成员都有一个父成员和零个或更多个子成员的方式组织维度成员的逻辑树结构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1144">A logical tree structure that organizes the members of a dimension such that each member has one parent member and zero or more child members.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1145">维度级别 (dimension level)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1145">dimension level</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1146">维度层次结构中成员集的名称，该集的所有成员与层次结构的根元素的距离相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1146">The name of a set of members in a dimension hierarchy such that all members of the set are at the same distance from the root of the hierarchy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1147">例如，时间层次结构可以包含年、月和日级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1147">For example, a time hierarchy may contain the levels Year, Month, and Day.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1148">维度成员 (dimension member)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1148">dimension member</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1149">维度中的单个位置或项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1149">A single position or item in a dimension.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1150">维度成员可以是用户定义的或预定义的，并且可具有与其相关联的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1150">Dimension members can be user-defined or predefined and can have properties associated with them.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1151">维度成员属性 (dimension member property)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1151">dimension member property</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1152">维度成员的特性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1152">A characteristic of a dimension member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1153">维度成员属性可以是字母数字、布尔值或日期/时间数据类型，并且可以是用户定义的或预定义的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1153">Dimension member properties can be alphanumeric, Boolean, or Date/Time data types, and can be user-defined or predefined.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1154">维度表 (dimension table)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1154">dimension table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1155">数据仓库中的一个表，其中的项描述事实数据表中的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1155">A table in a data warehouse whose entries describe data in a fact table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1156">直接连接 (direct connect)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1156">direct connect</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1157">连接到后端数据库的状态，因此在保存数据库关系图或其中的所选项时，对数据库关系图所做的任何更改会自动更新数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1157">The state of being connected to a back-end database, so that any changes you make to a database diagram automatically update your database when you save the diagram or selected items in it.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1160">脏页 (dirty page)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1160">dirty page</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1161">包含尚未写入磁盘的修改的缓冲区页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1161">A buffer page that contains modifications that have not been written to disk.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1162">脏读 (dirty read)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1162">dirty read</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1163">包含未提交数据的一种读取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1163">A read that contains uncommitted data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1164">已禁用的索引 (disabled index)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1164">disabled index</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1165">标记为已禁用的任何索引。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1165">Any index that has been marked as disabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1166">已禁用的索引不可由数据库引擎使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1166">A disabled index is unavailable for use by the database engine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1167">已禁用的索引的索引定义保留在没有基础索引数据的系统目录中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1167">The index definition of a disabled index remains in the system catalog with no underlying index data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1168">离散信号 (discrete signal)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1168">discrete signal</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1169">由数量序列构成的一种时序，此类时序是针对离散整数域的一种功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1169">A time series consisting of a sequence of quantities, that is a time series that is a function over a domain of discrete integers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1170">离散化 (discretize)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1170">discretize</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1171">将一组连续数据的值放入组中以便得到离散数目的可能状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1171">To put values of a continuous set of data into groups so that there are a discrete number of possible states.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1172">离散化列 (discretized column)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1172">discretized column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1173">表示有限、计数数据的列</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1173">A column that represents finite, counted data</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1174">非重复计数度量值 (distinct count measure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1174">distinct count measure</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1175">通常用于确定对于某个维度的每个成员，另一维度有多少不同的最低级别成员共享事实数据表中的行的一种度量值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1175">A measure commonly used to determine for each member of a dimension how many distinct, lowest-level members of another dimension share rows in the fact table.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1182">distribution cleanup agent</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1182">distribution cleanup agent</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1183">在 SQL Server 代理下运行的一种计划的作业。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1183">A scheduled job that runs under SQL Server Agent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1184">在所有订阅服务器都已接收了某一事务后，该代理将从分发数据库中删除该事务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1184">After all Subscribers have received a transaction, the agent removes the transaction from the distribution database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1185">它还在与快照文件相对应的条目已从分发数据库中删除后将这些文件从文件系统中清除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1185">It also cleans up snapshot files from the file system after entries corresponding to those files have been removed from the distribution database.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1218">休眠的会话 (dormant session)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1218">dormant session</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1219">处于预登录状态的会话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1219">Session in pre-login state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1220">可以启动或结束会话来修改它们的状态，但它们通常保留为“睡眠/空闲”状态（如会话已启动且在服务器上处于打开状态以供客户端使用时）或“休眠”状态（如会话已结束且当前在服务器上无法用于客户端时）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1220">Sessions can be initiated or ended to modify their state, but they generally remain in either a "sleep/idle" state, such as when the session has been initiated and is open at the server for client use; or a "dormant" state, such as when the session has been ended and the session is not currently available at the server for client use.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1221">双字节字符集 (double byte character set)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1221">double byte character set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1222">可使用多个字节来表示单个字符的字符集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1222">A character set that can use more than one byte to represent a single character.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1223">DBCS 包括某些由 1 个字节构成的字符以及某些由 2 个字节构成的字符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1223">A DBCS includes some characters that consist of 1 byte and some characters that consist of 2 bytes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1224">中文、日语和韩语等语言使用 DBCS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1224">Languages such as Chinese, Japanese, and Korean use DBCS.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1225">双字节字符集 (double-byte character set)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1225">double-byte character set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1226">可使用多个字节来表示单个字符的字符集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1226">A character set that can use more than one byte to represent a single character.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1227">DBCS 包括某些由 1 个字节构成的字符以及某些由 2 个字节构成的字符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1227">A DBCS includes some characters that consist of 1 byte and some characters that consist of 2 bytes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1228">中文、日语和韩语等语言使用 DBCS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1228">Languages such as Chinese, Japanese, and Korean use DBCS.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1231">仅下载类项目 (download-only article)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1231">download-only article</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1232">合并发布中只能在发布服务器或使用服务器订阅的订阅服务器上更新的项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1232">An article in a merge publication that can be updated only at the Publisher or at a Subscriber that uses a server subscription.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1233">DPM 客户端 (DPM Client)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1233">DPM Client</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1234">此 Data Protection Manager (DPM) 客户端使用户能够按照其备份管理员配置的公司保护策略保护和还原其数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1234">The Data Protection Manager (DPM) Client enables the user to protect and recover their data as per the company protection policy configured by their backup administrator.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1302">动态路由 (dynamic routing)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1302">dynamic routing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1303">自动调整为网络的当前状况的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1303">Routing that adjusts automatically to the current conditions of a network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1304">动态路由通常使用若干动态路由协议之一，例如路由信息协议 (RIP) 和边界网关协议 (BGP)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1304">Dynamic routing typically uses one of several dynamic-routing protocols such as Routing Information Protocol (RIP) and Border Gateway Protocol (BGP).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1305">请与静态路由进行比较。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1305">Compare static routing.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1306">动态快照 (dynamic snapshot)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1306">dynamic snapshot</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1307">在合并复制中，仅包含单个分区中的数据的快照。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1307">In merge replication, a snapshot that includes only the data from a single partition.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1410">排他锁 (exclusive lock)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1410">exclusive lock</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1411">一种锁，用来防止在事务结束时释放资源的原始锁之前，任何其他事务获取该资源的锁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1411">A lock that prevents any other transaction from acquiring a lock on a resource until the original lock on the resource is released at the end of the transaction.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1435">指数移动平均线 (exponential moving average)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1435">exponential moving average</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1436">移动平均线公式对一段时间内的最新数据赋予较大权重，较旧数据赋予较小权重。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1436">A moving average of data that gives more weight to the more recent data in the period and less weight to the older data in the period.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1437">该公式应用按指数规律减小的加权系数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1437">The formula applies weighting factors which decrease exponentially.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1438">每个较旧数据点的权重按指数规律减小，这为最近观察结果提供高得多的权重，但仍不会完全放弃较旧的观察结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1438">The weighting for each older data point decreases exponentially, giving much more importance to recent observations while still not discarding older observations entirely.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1491">故障转移群集 (failover cluster)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1491">failover cluster</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1492">位于一个位置中的一组服务器，它们联网在一起以便在其中一台服务器发生故障时提供实时备份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1492">A group of servers that are in one location and that are networked together for the purpose of providing live backup in case one of the servers fails.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1493">故障转移群集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1493">failover clustering</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1494">一个高可用性进程，在其中，在一台计算机上运行的应用程序或服务的实例可以在第一台计算机发生故障时故障转移到故障转移群集中的另一台计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1494">A high availability process in which an instance of an application or a service, running over one machine, can fail-over onto another machine in the failover cluster in the case the first one fails.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1495">故障转移伙伴 (failover partner)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1495">failover partner</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1496">在与伙伴服务器的连接失败时使用的服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1496">The server used if the connection to the partner server fails.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1501">严重错误 (fatal error)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1501">fatal error</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1502">导致系统或程序突然失败并且没有希望恢复的一种错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1502">An error that causes the system or a program to fail abruptly with no hope of recovery.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1503">灾难性错误的一个例子是无法处理的未捕获的异常。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1503">An example of a fatal error is an uncaught exception that cannot be handled.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1504">联合数据库服务器 (federated database servers)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1504">federated database servers</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1505">通过承载分布式分区视图的不同部分来分担数据处理负荷的一组相连服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1505">A set of linked servers that shares the processing load of data by hosting partitions of a distributed partitioned view.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1510">纤程模式 (fiber mode)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1510">fiber mode</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1511">SQL Server 实例为每个 SQL 计划程序分配一个 Windows 线程，然后为每个工作线程分配一个纤程（工作线程数不能超过 max worker threads 选项中设置的值）的一种情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1511">A situation where an instance of SQL Server allocates one Windows thread per SQL scheduler, and then allocates one fiber per worker thread, up to the value set in the max worker threads option.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1522">文件差异备份 (file differential backup)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1522">file differential backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1523">只包含自最新文件备份以来对每个文件所做更改的一个或多个文件的备份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1523">A backup of one or more files containing only changes made to each file since its most recent file backup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1524">文件差异备份需要以完整文件备份为基础。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1524">A file differential backup requires a full file backup as a base.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1543">筛选器遗忘知识 (filter forgotten knowledge)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1543">filter forgotten knowledge</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1544">用作筛选器跟踪起点的知识。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1544">The knowledge that is used as the starting point for filter tracking.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1545">筛选器跟踪副本可以通过删除虚影并提前了解筛选器遗忘知识，以包含已被删除的虚影的最高版本，从而节省存储空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1545">A filter-tracking replica can save storage space by removing ghosts and advancing the filter forgotten knowledge to contain the highest version of the ghosts that have been removed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1546">筛选键 (filter key)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1546">filter key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1547">在筛选键映射中映射为筛选器的 4 字节的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1547">A 4-byte value that maps to a filter in a filter key map.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1552">细粒度锁 (fine-grained lock)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1552">fine-grained lock</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1553">适用于少量代码或数据的锁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1553">A lock that applies to a small amount of code or data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1554">适合 (fit)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1554">fit</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1555">用于评估数据挖掘算法是否成功的条件之一。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1555">One of the criteria used for evaluating the success of a data mining algorithm.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1556">适合通常表示为 0 和 1 之间的值，并且通过取评估的事例的预测值和实际值之间的协方差并且除以相同预测值和实际值的标准方差进行计算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1556">Fit is typically represented as a value between 0 and 1, and is calculated by taking the covariance between the predicted and actual values of evaluated cases and dividing by the standard deviations of the same predicted and actual values.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1557">固定数据库角色 (fixed database role)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1557">fixed database role</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1558">每个数据库中都存在的预定义角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1558">A predefined role that exists in each database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1559">该角色的作用域仅限于在其中定义该角色的数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1559">The scope of the role is limited to the database in which it is defined.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1560">固定服务器角色 (fixed server role)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1560">fixed server role</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1561">存在于服务器级别的预定义角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1561">A predefined role that exists at the server level.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1562">该角色的作用域仅限于在其中定义该角色的 SQL Server 实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1562">The scope of the role is limited to the SQL Server instance in which it is defined.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1579">折叠计数 (fold count)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1579">fold count</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1580">表示将在原始数据集中创建的分区数的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1580">A value that represents the number of partitions that will be created within the original data set.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1581">文件夹层次结构 (folder hierarchy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1581">folder hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1582">绑定的命名空间，用来唯一标识在报表服务器上存储并由其管理的所有报表、文件夹、共享数据源项和资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1582">A bounded namespace that uniquely identifies all reports, folders, shared data source items, and resources that are stored in and managed by a report server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1583">强制服务 (forced service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1583">forced service</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1584">在数据库镜像会话中，是指在负责将服务传输到镜像数据库（但它处于未知状态）的主体服务器出现故障时数据库所有者启动的故障转移。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1584">In a database mirroring session, a failover initiated by the database owner upon the failure of the principal server that transfers service to the mirror database while it is in an unknown state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1585">数据可能丢失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1585">Data may be lost.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1586">外键 (foreign key)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1586">foreign key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1587">某一数据库表中来自另一个表（也称作“被引用表”）的键，并且其值匹配该被引用表中的主键 (PK) 或唯一键。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1587">A key in a database table that comes from another table (also know as the "referenced table") and whose values match the primary key (PK) or unique key in the referenced table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1588">外键关联 (foreign key association)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1588">foreign key association</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1589">实体之间的关联，通过外键属性进行管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1589">An association between entities that is managed through foreign key properties.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1590">外表 (foreign table)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1590">foreign table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1591">包含外键的表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1591">A table that contains a foreign key.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1592">格式化文件 (format file)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1592">format file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1593">包含元信息（例如数据类型和列大小）的文件，用于在从数据文件中读取数据或者向其中写入数据时解释数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1593">A file containing meta information (such as data type and column size) that is used to interpret data when being read from or written to a data file.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1594">只进游标 (forward-only cursor)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1594">forward-only cursor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1595">不能滚动的游标；只能按照从第一行到最后一行的顺序读取行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1595">A cursor that cannot be scrolled; rows can be read only in sequence from the first row to the last row.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1596">自由格式语言 (free-form language)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1596">free-form language</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1597">其语法不受到行上字符位置的约束的一种语言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1597">A language whose syntax is not constrained by the position of characters on a line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1598">C 和 Pascal 是自由格式语言，FORTRAN 则不是。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1598">C and Pascal are free-form languages; FORTRAN is not.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1599">完整备份 (full backup)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1599">full backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1600">整个数据库的备份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1600">A backup of an entire database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1601">完整差异备份 (full differential backup)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1601">full differential backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1602">数据库中所有文件的备份，只包含自最新完整备份以来对数据库所做的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1602">A backup of all files in the database, containing only changes made to the database since the most recent full backup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1603">完整差异备份需要以完整备份为基础。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1603">A full differential backup requires a full backup as a base.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1604">完全外部联接 (full outer join)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1604">full outer join</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1605">一种外部联接，这种联接中包括所有联接表中的所有行，无论它们是否匹配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1605">A type of outer join in which all rows in all joined tables are included, whether they are matched or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1606">例如，书名和出版商之间的完全外部联接显示所有书名和所有出版商，甚至包括那些没有匹配值的行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1606">For example, a full outer join between titles and publishers shows all titles and all publishers, even those that have no match.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1607">完整恢复模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1607">full recovery model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1608">一种数据库恢复模式，其中完整记录所有事务，并保留所有日志记录直至对它们进行备份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1608">A database recovery mode that fully logs all transactions and retains all the log records until after they are backed up.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1609">如果在失败后备份了日志尾部，则数据库可恢复到失败点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1609">The database can be recovered to the point of failure if the tail of the log is backed up after the failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1610">支持所有形式的恢复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1610">All forms of recovery are supported.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1611">全文目录 (full-text catalog)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1611">full-text catalog</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1612">全文索引组件以及在特定的目录结构中组织并且包含执行查询所需数据的其他文件的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1612">A collection of full-text index components and other files that are organized in a specific directory structure and contain the data that is needed to perform queries.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1613">全文启用 (full-text enabling)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1613">full-text enabling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1614">允许在当前数据库上发生全文查询的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1614">The process of allowing full-text querying to occur on the current database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1615">全文查询 (full-text query)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1615">full-text query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1616">一种 SELECT 语句，在基于字符的列（数据类型为 char、varchar、text、ntext、nchar 或 nvarchar）中搜索词、短语、或者词或短语的多种形式的查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1616">As a SELECT statement, a query that searches for words, phrases, or multiple forms of a word or phrase in the character-based columns (of char, varchar, text, ntext, nchar, or nvarchar data types).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1617">这种 SELECT 语句返回满足搜索条件的行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1617">The SELECT statement returns those rows meeting the search criteria.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1618">全文搜索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1618">full-text search</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1619">根据所有实际的文本数据，而不是根据包含一组有限关键字的索引来搜索一个或多个文档、记录或字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1619">A search for one or more documents, records, or strings based on all of the actual text data rather than on an index containing a limited set of keywords.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1620">全文服务 (Full-Text service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1620">Full-Text service</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1621">执行全文查询的 SQL Server 组件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1621">The SQL Server component that performs the full-text querying.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1622">全角字符 (full-width character)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1622">full-width character</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1623">在双字节字符集中，由 2 个字节表示并且通常具有半角差异的字符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1623">In a double-byte character set, a character that is represented by 2 bytes and typically has a half-width variant.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1624">函数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1624">function</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1625">作为单个逻辑单元运行的代码块。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1625">A piece of code that operates as a single logical unit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1626">函数通过名称来调用，接受可选输入参数，并返回状态和可选输出参数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1626">A function is called by name, accepts optional input parameters, and returns a status and optional output parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1627">许多编程语言都支持函数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1627">Many programming languages support functions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1628">模糊分组 (fuzzy grouping)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1628">fuzzy grouping</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1629">Integration Services 中的一种数据清除方法，该方法检查数据集中的值，并确定相关数据行组和作为组的规范表示形式的一个数据行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1629">In Integration Services, a data cleaning methodology that examines values in a dataset and identifies groups of related data rows and the one data row that is the canonical representation of the group.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1630">模糊匹配 (fuzzy matching)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1630">fuzzy matching</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1631">Integration Services 中的一种查找方法，它使用近似匹配算法来找到引用表中相似的数据值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1631">In Integration Services, a lookup methodology that uses an approximate matching algorithm to locate similar data values in a reference table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1632">GAC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1632">GAC</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1633">计算机范围内的代码缓存，用于存储专为由计算机上的许多应用程序共享而安装的程序集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1633">A computer-wide code cache that stores assemblies specifically installed to be shared by many applications on the computer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1634">间隙深度 (gap depth)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1634">gap depth</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1635">指定沿着不同行显示的数据序列之间的距离作为分簇结果的一种度量方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1635">A measure that specifies the distance between data series that are displayed along distinct rows, as a result of clustering.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1636">垃圾收集 (garbage collection)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1636">garbage collection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1637">自动恢复堆内存的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1637">A process for automatic recovery of heap memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1638">将释放已分配但不再使用的内存块，并且可移动仍在使用中的内存块以便将可用内存合并到更大的块中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1638">Blocks of memory that had been allocated but are no longer in use are freed, and blocks of memory still in use may be moved to consolidate the free memory into larger blocks.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1639">垃圾收集器 (garbage collector)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1639">garbage collector</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1640">操作系统中执行垃圾收集的部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1640">The part of the operating system that performs garbage collection.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1641">门链接 (gated link)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1641">gated link</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1642">两个或多个对象之间受保护的链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1642">A protected link between two or more objects.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1643">在执行期间，一旦已建立对象关系，则不跨越该对象关系检查权限，并且不必多次检查凭据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1643">During execution, permissions are not checked across the object relationship once it has been established and credentials don't have to be checked several times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1644">如果向很多依赖性对象授权是不合适或不可管理的，则需要使用此类型的链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1644">This type of link is useful when it is not appropriate or manageable to give permissions to many dependent objects.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1645">聚集-写入操作 (gather-write operation)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1645">gather-write operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1646">数据库引擎将多个修改的数据页收集到单个写入操作中的一种性能优化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1646">A performance optimization where the Database Engine collects multiple modified data pages into a single write operation.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1647">GC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1647">GC</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1648">自动恢复堆内存的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1648">A process for automatic recovery of heap memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1649">将释放已分配但不再使用的内存块，并且可移动仍在使用中的内存块以便将可用内存合并到更大的块中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1649">Blocks of memory that had been allocated but are no longer in use are freed, and blocks of memory still in use may be moved to consolidate the free memory into larger blocks.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1650">生成的代码 (generated code)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1650">generated code</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1651">在 RIA 服务链接在服务器和客户端项目之间存在时，基于在中间层公开的操作和实体为客户端项目自动生成的代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1651">Code that is automatically generated for the client project based on operations and entities exposed in the middle tier when a RIA Services link exists between the server and client projects.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1652">生成器 (generator)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1652">generator</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1653">将事件与订阅进行匹配并生成通知的 Notification Services 的组件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1653">The component of Notification Services that matches events to subscriptions and produces notifications.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1654">地理数据 (geographic data)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1654">geographic data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1655">存储诸如 GPS 纬度和经度坐标之类的椭球体（圆形地球）数据的一种空间数据类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1655">A type of spatial data that stores ellipsoidal (round-earth) data, such as GPS latitude and longitude coordinates.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1656">几何图形数据 (geometric data)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1656">geometric data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1657">支持平面或欧几里得（平面球）数据的一种空间数据类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1657">A type of spatial data that supports planar, or Euclidean (flat-earth), data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1658">虚影 (ghost)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1658">ghost</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1659">筛选副本中原先位于筛选器中但已移出的项或变更单位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1659">An item or change unit in a filtered replica that was in the filter and has moved out.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1660">虚影记录 (ghost record)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1660">ghost record</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1661">叶级索引中已标记为要删除但尚未由数据库引擎删除的行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1661">Row in the leaf level of an index that has been marked for deletion, but has not yet been deleted by the database engine.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1662">虚影行 (ghost row)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1662">ghost row</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1663">叶级索引中已标记为要删除但尚未由数据库引擎删除的行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1663">Row in the leaf level of an index that has been marked for deletion, but has not yet been deleted by the database engine.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1664">全局程序集缓存 (global assembly cache)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1664">global assembly cache</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1665">计算机范围内的代码缓存，用于存储专为由计算机上的许多应用程序共享而安装的程序集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1665">A computer-wide code cache that stores assemblies specifically installed to be shared by many applications on the computer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1666">全局默认值 (global default)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1666">global default</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1667">为特定数据库定义并由不同表的列共享的默认值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1667">A default that is defined for a specific database and is shared by columns of different tables.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1725">高可用性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1725">high availability</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1726">系统或设备在需要时可用的一种能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1726">The ability of a system or device to be usable when it is needed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1727">如果用百分比的形式表示，则高可用性是实际服务时间除以所需服务时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1727">When expressed as a percentage, high availability is the actual service time divided by the required service time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1728">尽管高可用性不会确保系统将不停机，但如果实现 99.999% 的网络正常运行时间，则网络通常被视作具备高可用性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1728">Although high availability does not guarantee that a system will have no downtime, a network often is considered highly available if it achieves 99.999 percent network uptime.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1729">高水印 (high watermark)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1729">high watermark</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1730">针对每个缓存主机的内存使用量阈值，它指定何时将对象从内存中逐出，直至内存使用量下降回低水印，而与对象是否到期无关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1730">A memory consumption threshold on each cache host that specifies when objects are evicted out of memory, regardless of whether they have expired or not, until memory consumption goes back down to the low watermark.</span></span>|

For every P time unit a new window of size L is created.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1832">初始同步 (initial synchronization)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1832">initial synchronization</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1833">订阅的首次同步。在此过程中会将复制所需的系统表和其他对象以及每个项目的架构和数据复制到订阅服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1833">The first synchronization for a subscription, during which system tables and other objects that are required by replication, and the schema and data for each article, are copied to the Subscriber.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1834">起始磁带 (initial tape)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1834">initial tape</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1835">使用磁带备份设备的介质集中，介质簇中的第一个磁带。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1835">In a media set using tape backup devices, the first tape in a media family.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1836">内部联接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1836">inner join</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1837">通过比较源表间共享的列的值，从多个源表检索行的操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1837">An operation that retrieves rows from multiple source tables by comparing the values from columns shared between the source tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1838">内部联接排除在其他源表中没有匹配行的源表中的行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1838">An inner join excludes rows from a source table that have no matching rows in the other source tables.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1839">亲身身份验证 (in-person authentication)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1839">in-person authentication</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1840">用于完成证书请求事务的物理身份验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1840">Physical authentication to complete a certificate request transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1841">例如，请求解锁其个人标识号 (PIN) 的最终用户将亲自拜访其证书管理员，并且提供含有标识（例如员工徽章或驱动程序许可证）的亲身身份验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1841">For example, an end user requesting his/her personal identification number (PIN) be unblocked will visit a certificate manager in person to provide in-person authentication with identification, such as an employee badge or drivers license.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1842">InProc</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1842">InProc</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1843">一种情况，其中，COM 对象的代码从 DLL 文件加载并且位于与客户端相同的进程中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1843">A circumstance where the COM object's code is loaded from a DLL file and is located in the same process as the client.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1844">输入适配器 (input adapter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1844">input adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1845">从外部源（如数据库、文件、股票资讯、网络端口、制造设备等）接受传入事件流的一种适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1845">An adapter that accepts incoming event streams from external sources such as databases, files, ticker feeds, network ports, manufacturing devices and so on.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1846">输入成员 (input member)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1846">input member</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1847">其值直接从数据源加载而不是从其他数据计算得到的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1847">A member whose value is loaded directly from the data source instead of being calculated from other data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1848">输入集 (input set)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1848">input set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1849">提供给多维表达式 (MDX) 值表达式的数据集，表达式使用这些数据进行运算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1849">The set of data provided to a Multidimensional Expressions (MDX) value expression upon which the expression operates.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1850">输入源 (input source)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1850">input source</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1851">用作查询的信息源的任何表、视图或架构关系图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1851">Any table, view, or schema diagram used as an information source for a query.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1852">输入流 (input stream)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1852">input stream</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1853">在程序中用作与特定任务或目标相关联的字节序列的一种信息流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1853">A flow of information used in a program as a sequence of bytes that are associated with a particular task or destination.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1854">输入流包括从键盘到内存读取的字符序列以及从磁盘文件读取的数据块。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1854">Input streams include series of characters read from the keyboard to memory and blocks of data read from disk files.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1855">不感知游标 (insensitive cursor)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1855">insensitive cursor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1856">一种打开时不反映其他用户对基础数据所做的数据修改的游标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1856">A cursor that does not reflect data modification made to the underlying data by other users while the cursor is open.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1857">插入事件 (insert event)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1857">insert event</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1858">用于表示事件到达流中的事件类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1858">The event kind used to signify the arrival of an event into the stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1859">插入事件类型由定义事件有效生命周期的元数据和事件的负载（数据）字段构成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1859">The insert event type consists of metadata that defines the valid lifetime of the event and the payload (data) fields of the event.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1860">插入查询 (Insert Into query)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1860">Insert Into query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1861">将来自一个表的特定列和行复制到另一个表或同一个表中的查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1861">A query that copies specific columns and rows from one table to another or to the same table.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1864">instance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1864">instance</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1865">计算机上运行的 SQL Server 副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1865">A copy of SQL Server running on a computer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1866">实例控制提供程序 (instance control provider)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1866">instance control provider</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1867">一种提供程序，可用于针对实例存储区中的工作流实例发出控制命令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1867">A provider that allows you to issue control commands against workflow instances in an instance store.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1868">例如，您可以使用 SQL 控制提供程序挂起、恢复或终止在 SQL Server 数据库中存储的实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1868">For example, a SQL control provider lets you suspend, resume, or terminate instances stored in a SQL Server database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1869">在您执行控制实例存储区中的工作流实例的某一 cmdlet 时，该 cmdlet 在内部将该控制提供程序用于该实例存储区，以便向该实例发送命令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1869">When you execute a cmdlet that controls a workflow instance in an instance store, the cmdlet internally uses the control provider for that instance store to send commands to the instance.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1870">实例查询提供程序 (instance query provider)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1870">instance query provider</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1871">一种提供程序，可用于针对实例存储区发出查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1871">A provider that allows you to issue queries against an instance store.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1872">例如，SQL 查询提供程序允许针对 SQL Server 数据库中存储的工作流实例进行的查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1872">For example, a SQL query provider lets you query for workflow instances stored in a SQL Server database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1873">在您执行针对实例存储区查询实例的某一 cmdlet 时，该 cmdlet 在内部使用查询提供程序从该存储区中检索实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1873">When you execute a cmdlet that queries for instances against an instance store, the cmdlet internally uses the query provider to retrieve instances from that store.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1876">实例存储区提供程序 (instance store provider)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1876">instance store provider</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1877">在 Windows AppFabric 中，指的是可用于创建实例存储区对象的一种提供程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1877">In Windows AppFabric, a provider that allows you to create instance store objects.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1878">例如，SQL 存储区提供程序允许客户端创建 SQL 工作流实例存储区对象，而后者又允许客户端将工作流实例保存到持久性存储区中以及从持久性存储区中检索工作流实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1878">For example, a SQL store provider allows clients to create SQL workflow instance store objects, which in turn allows clients to save and retrieve workflow instances to and from a persistence store.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1879">集成</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1879">integration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1880">在计算中，指的是将不同的活动、程序或硬件组件组合到一个功能单元中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1880">In computing, the combining of different activities, programs, or hardware components into a functional unit.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1881">完整性 (integrity)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1881">integrity</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1882">数据的精确性并且其符合其预期值，特别是在传输或处理后。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1882">The accuracy of data and its conformity to its expected value, especially after being transmitted or processed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1883">完整性约束 (integrity constraint)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1883">integrity constraint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1884">为表定义的属性，防止可能创建无效数据的数据修改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1884">A property defined on a table that prevents data modifications that would create invalid data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1885">意向锁 (intent lock)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1885">intent lock</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1886">放置在资源层次结构的某个级别上的锁，以保护较低级别资源上的共享锁或排他锁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1886">A lock that is placed on one level of a resource hierarchy to protect shared or exclusive locks on lower-level resources.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1889">交互式结构化查询语言 (interactive structured query language)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1889">interactive structured query language</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1890">SQL Server 提供的交互式命令提示实用工具，使用户可以从服务器或工作站运行 Transact-SQL 语句或批处理并查看返回的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1890">An interactive command prompt utility provided with SQL Server that lets users run Transact-SQL statements or batches from a server or workstation and view the results that are returned.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1891">interface</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1891">interface</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1892">一组定义的属性、方法和集合，构成行为和数据的逻辑分组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1892">A defined set of properties, methods, and collections that form a logical grouping of behaviors and data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1893">接口隐含 (interface implication)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1893">interface implication</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1894">如果一个接口隐含另一个接口，则实现第一个接口的任何类还必须实现第二个接口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1894">If an interface implies another interface, then any class that implements the first interface must also implement the second interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1895">接口隐含用于信息模型中来获得多重继承的某些效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1895">Interface implication is used in an information model to get some of the effects of multiple inheritance.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1896">中间语言 (Intermediate Language)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1896">intermediate language</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1897">用作原始源语言（通常是高级语言）和目标语言（通常是机器代码）之间的中间步骤的一种计算机语言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1897">A computer language used as an intermediate step between the original source language, usually a high-level language, and the target language, usually machine code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1898">某些高级编译器使用汇编语言作为中间语言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1898">Some high-level compilers use assembly language as an intermediate language.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1899">国际电工委员会 (International Electrotechnical Commission)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1899">International Electrotechnical Commission</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1900">负责开发国际数据通信标准的两个国际标准组织之一。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1900">One of two international standards bodies responsible for developing international data communications standards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1901">国际电工委员会 (IEC) 与国际标准化组织 (ISO) 密切合作来定义计算标准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1901">The International Electrotechnical Commission (IEC) works closely with the International Organization for Standardization (ISO) to define standards of computing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1902">它们共同发布了 SQL 的 ISO/IEC SQL-92 标准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1902">They jointly published the ISO/IEC SQL-92 standard for SQL.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1903">Internet 协议安全 (Internet Protocol security)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1903">Internet Protocol security</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1904">一组符合行业标准、基于加密的服务和协议，可帮助保护网络上数据的安全。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1904">A set of industry-standard, cryptography-based services and protocols that help to protect data over a network.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1905">进程间通信 (interprocess communication)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1905">interprocess communication</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1906">一个任务或进程与多任务操作系统中的其他任务或进程进行通信的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1906">The ability of one task or process to communicate with another in a multitasking operating system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1907">常见的方法包括管道、信号量、共享内存、队列、信号和邮箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1907">Common methods include pipes, semaphores, shared memory, queues, signals, and mailboxes.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1908">间隔事件 (interval event)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1908">interval event</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1909">其负载在给定的时间段内有效的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1909">An event whose payload is valid for a given period of time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1910">间隔事件的元数据要求在事件元数据中同时提供间隔的开始时间和结束时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1910">The metadata of the interval event requires that both the start and end time of the interval be provided in the event metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1911">间隔事件只在此特定间隔内有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1911">Interval events are valid only for this specific interval.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1912">间隔事件模型 (interval event model)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1912">interval event model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1913">间隔事件的事件模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1913">The event model of an interval event.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1916">IP 地址</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1916">IP address</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1917">出于通过传输数据包进行通信目的唯一标识连接到 Internet 的主机（计算机）与其他 Internet 主机的二进制编号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1917">A binary number that uniquely identifies a host (computer) connected to the Internet to other Internet hosts, for the purposes of communication through the transfer of packets.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1979">键范围锁 (key range lock)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1979">key range lock</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1980">用于锁定表中记录之间范围的锁，以防止对一组记录进行虚拟添加或虚拟删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1980">A lock that is used to lock ranges between records in a table to prevent phantom additions to, or deletions from, a set of records.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1981">它确保可序列化事务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1981">Ensures serializable transactions.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1996">KRA</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1996">KRA</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1997">与证书管理员合作来恢复用户的私钥的指定用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1997">A designated user that works with a certificate administrator to recover a user's private key.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1998">一个特定的证书模板将应用于密钥恢复代理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1998">A specific certificate template is applied to a Key Recovery Agent.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-1999">非 Unicode 程序的语言 (Language for non-Unicode programs)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-1999">Language for non-Unicode programs</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2000">一个“区域和语言选项”设置，为特定计算机指定默认代码页和关联的位图字体文件，此设置影响特定计算机的所有用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2000">A Regional and Language Options setting that specifies the default code pages and associated bitmap font files for a specific computer that affects all of that computer's users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2001">通过指定默认代码页和字体，为一种操作系统语言版本编写的非 Unicode 应用程序可以直接在其他操作系统语言版本上正确运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2001">The default code pages and fonts enable a non-Unicode application written for one operating system language version to run correctly on another operating system language version.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2002">语言服务分析器 (language service parser)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2002">language service parser</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2003">用于描述源代码中标记的功能和范围的组件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2003">A component that is used to describe the functions and scope of the tokens in source code.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2007">闩锁 (latch)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2007">latch</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2008">一种短期的同步对象保护操作，此类操作无需为事务的整个生命周期锁定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2008">A short-term synchronization object protecting actions that need not be locked for the life of a transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2009">闩锁主要用于保护存储引擎主动从基表或索引传输到关系引擎的行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2009">A latch is primarily used to protect a row that the storage engine is actively transferring from a base table or index to the relational engine.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2081">日志链 (log chain)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2081">log chain</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2082">数据库的一组连续的事务日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2082">A continuous sequence of transaction logs for a database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2083">新日志链以创建数据库后生成的第一个日志备份开始，或者从数据库从简单模式切换到完整模式或大容量日志恢复模式时生成的第一个日志备份开始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2083">A new log chain begins with the first backup taken after the database is created, or when the database is switched from the simple to the full or bulk-logged recovery model.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2084">日志链在恢复之后的某一还原后分叉，并且创建新的恢复分支。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2084">A log chain forks after a restore followed by a recovery, creating a new recovery branch.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2085">日志提供程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2085">log provider</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2086">一种在运行时记录包信息的提供程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2086">A provider that logs package information at run time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2087">Integration Services 包括多种日志提供程序，可实现在包执行过程中捕获事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2087">Integration Services includes a variety of log providers that make it possible to capture events during package execution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2088">日志可以多种格式创建和存储，例如 XML、文本、数据库或 Windows 事件日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2088">Logs are created and stored in formats such as XML, text, database, or in the Windows event log.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2089">日志读取器代理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2089">Log Reader Agent</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2090">复制中使用的可执行文件，用来监视为事务复制配置的每个数据库的事务，并将已为复制标记的事务从事务复制到分发数据库中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2090">In Replication, the executable that monitors the transaction of each database configured for transactional replication, and copies the transactions marked for replication from the transaction into the distribution database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2091">日志序列号 (log sequence number)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2091">log sequence number</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2092">分配给事务日志中的每个项的唯一编号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2092">A unique number assigned to each entry in a transaction log.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2093">系统将根据创建实体的顺序依次分配 LSN。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2093">LSNs are assigned sequentially according to the order in which entries are created.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2094">日志传送</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2094">log shipping</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2095">以设定间隔将日志备份从读/写数据库（主数据库）复制到一个或多个远程服务器实例（辅助服务器）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2095">Copying, at regular intervals, log backup from a read-write database (the primary database) to one or more remote server instances (secondary servers).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2096">每个辅助服务器都具有通过还原主数据库的完整备份（而不恢复）而创建的称作辅助数据库的只读数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2096">Each secondary server has a read-only database, called a secondary database, that was created by restoring a full backup of the primary database without recovery.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2097">辅助服务器将每个复制的日志备份还原到辅助数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2097">The secondary server restores each copied log backup to the secondary database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2098">辅助服务器是用于主服务器的热备用服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2098">The secondary servers are warm standbys for the primary server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2099">日志传送配置 (log shipping configuration)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2099">log shipping configuration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2100">单个主服务器、一个或多个辅助服务器（每个服务器均有一个辅助数据库）和一个监视服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2100">A single primary server, one or more secondary servers (each with a secondary database), and a monitor server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2101">日志传送操作 (log shipping job)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2101">log shipping job</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2102">执行下列日志传送操作之一的作业：备份主服务器上主数据库的事务日志（备份作业）、将事务日志文件复制到辅助服务器（复制作业）或将日志备份还原到辅助服务器上的辅助数据库（还原作业）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2102">A job performing one of the following log-shipping operations: backing up the transaction log of the primary database at the primary server (the backup job), copying the transaction log file to a secondary server (the copy job), or restoring the log backup to the secondary database on a secondary server (the restore job).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2103">备份作业驻留在主服务器上，复制和还原作业驻留各辅助服务器上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2103">The backup job resides on the primary server; the copy and restore jobs reside on each of the secondary servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2104">另请参阅：主数据库、主服务器、辅助数据库、辅助服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2104">See also: primary database, primary server, secondary database, secondary server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2105">日志接收器 (log sink)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2105">log sink</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2106">缓存客户端和缓存主机的跟踪功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2106">A tracing function of the cache client and cache host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2107">日志接收器从缓存客户端或缓存主机捕获跟踪事件，并且可以在控制台显示这些跟踪事件、将它们写入某一日志文件或者将它们报告给 Windows 中的 Windows 事件跟踪 (ETW) 框架。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2107">Log sinks capture trace events from the cache client or cache host and can display them in a console, write them to a log file, or report them to the Event Tracing for Windows (ETW) framework inside Windows.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2108">逻辑错误 (logic error)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2108">logic error</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2109">诸如错误算法等此类错误，可导致程序生成不正确的结果，但不会阻止程序运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2109">An error, such as a faulty algorithm, that causes a program to produce incorrect results but does not prevent the program from running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2110">因此，逻辑错误通常很难发现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2110">Consequently, a logic error is often very difficult to find.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2111">逻辑名称 (logical name)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2111">logical name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2112">SQL Server 用来标识文件的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2112">A name used by SQL Server to identify a file.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2113">逻辑记录 (logical record)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2113">logical record</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2114">一项合并复制功能，您可以使用此功能来定义不同表中相关行之间的关系，以便将这些行作为一个单元来处理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2114">A merge replication feature that allows you to define a relationship between related rows in different tables so that the rows are processed as a unit.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2120">长分析 (long parsing)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2120">long parsing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2121">在 SQL 系统中，有两种类型的线程：一是短线程，即短期占用资源的进程；另一种是长线程，即长期占用资源的进程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2121">In the SQL system there are two typical types of threads: - short thread: it is a process that use the resources for a short time and - long thread: it is a process that use the resources for a long time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2122">长分析就是对长期存在的线程进行分析。注：长/短的定义基于系统针对每个进程进行的计算/统计信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2122">long parsing: is the analysis of the threads that lived for a long time Note: the definition of short/long is based on the system calculation/statistic for each process.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2123">低框 (Low Box)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2123">Low Box</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2124">盒须图上框的最低值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2124">The lowest value of a box on a Box Plot chart.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2153">手动故障转移 (manual failover)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2153">manual failover</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2154">在数据库镜像会话中，是指在负责将服务从主体数据库传输到镜像数据库（处于同步状态）的主体服务器仍在运行时数据库所有者启动的故障转移。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2154">In a database mirroring session, a failover initiated by the database owner, while the principal server is still running, that transfers service from the principal database to the mirror database while they are in a synchronized state.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2155">多对多维度 (many-to-many dimension)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2155">many-to-many dimension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2156">维度和度量值组之间的一种关系，在这种关系中，一个事实数据可与多个维度成员关联，而一个维度成员也可以与多个事实数据关联。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2156">A relationship between a dimension and a measure group in which a single fact may be associated with many dimension members and a single dimension member may be associated with a many facts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2157">若要在维度与事实数据表之间定义这一关系，该维度应联接到中间事实数据表，反过来，此中间事实数据表应联接到已联接到此事实数据表的中间维度表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2157">To define this relationship between the dimension and the fact table, the dimension is joined to an intermediate fact table and the intermediate fact table is joined, in turn, to an intermediate dimension table that is joined to the fact table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2158">多对一关系 (many-to-one relationship)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2158">many-to-one relationship</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2159">这样的两个表之间的关系：一个表中的一个行可以与另一个表中的许多行相关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2159">A relationship between two tables in which one row in one table can relate to many rows in another table.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2174">地图视区 (map viewport)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2174">map viewport</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2175">要在地图报表项中显示的地图区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2175">The area of the map to display in the map report item.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2176">例如，针对整个美国的地图可能嵌入在某一报表中，但只显示针对西北各州的区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2176">For example, a map for the entire United States might be embedded in a report, but only the area for the northwestern states are displayed.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2216">MBCS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2216">MBCS</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2217">混合宽度的字符集，其中某些字符包含 1 个以上的字节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2217">A mixed-width character set, in which some characters consist of more than 1 byte.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2218">MBCS 用于日语、中文和韩语等语言，在这些语言中，256 个单字节字符集的可能值不足以表示所有可能的字符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2218">An MBCS is used in languages such as Japanese, Chinese, and Korean, where the 256 possible values of a single-byte character set are not sufficient to represent all possible characters.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2240">中值 (median)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2240">median</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2241">一组有序数值的中间值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2241">The middle value in a set of ordered numbers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2242">中值是通过选择最小值以使这组数值中至少有一半值不大于所选的值来确定的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2242">The median value is determined by choosing the smallest value such that at least half of the values in the set are no greater than the chosen value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2243">如果这组数值的个数为奇数，则中值对应于单个值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2243">If the number of values within the set is odd, the median value corresponds to a single value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2244">如果这组数值的个数为偶数，则中值对应于两个中间值的和除以 2 所得的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2244">If the number of values within the set is even, the median value corresponds to the sum of the two middle values divided by two.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2245">平均价公式 (median price formula)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2245">median price formula</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2246">计算最高价和最低价的平均值的公式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2246">A formula that calculates the average of the high and low prices.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2247">中值 (median value)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2247">median value</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2248">一组有序数值的中间值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2248">The middle value in a set of ordered numbers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2249">中值是通过选择最小值以使这组数值中至少有一半值不大于所选的值来确定的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2249">The median value is determined by choosing the smallest value such that at least half of the values in the set are no greater than the chosen value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2250">如果这组数值的个数为奇数，则中值对应于单个值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2250">If the number of values within the set is odd, the median value corresponds to a single value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2251">如果这组数值的个数为偶数，则中值对应于两个中间值的和除以 2 所得的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2251">If the number of values within the set is even, the median value corresponds to the sum of the two middle values divided by two.</span></span>|
