|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2335">挖掘模型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2335">mining model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2336">包含数据挖掘进程定义和定型活动结果的对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2336">An object that contains the definition of a data mining process and the results of the training activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2337">例如，数据挖掘模型可以指定进程的输入、输出、算法以及其他属性，并保留在定型活动（如决策树）期间收集的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2337">For example, a data mining model may specify the input, output, algorithm, and other properties of the process and hold the information gathered during the training activity, such as a decision tree.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2338">挖掘结构 (mining structure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2338">mining structure</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2339">用于定义生成挖掘模型所基于的数据域的数据挖掘对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2339">A data mining object that defines the data domain from which the mining models are built.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2340">次要刻度线 (minor tick mark)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2340">minor tick mark</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2341">与轴上的次要刻度单位对应的刻度线。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2341">A tick mark that corresponds to a minor scaling unit on an axis.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2342">镜像数据库 (mirror database)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2342">mirror database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2343">在数据库镜像会话中，通常与主体数据库完全同步的数据库副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2343">In a database mirroring session, the copy of the database that is normally fully synchronized with the principal database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2344">镜像服务器 (mirror server)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2344">mirror server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2345">在数据库镜像配置中，镜像数据库所在的服务器实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2345">In a database mirroring configuration, the server instance where the mirror database resides.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2346">镜像服务器是镜像伙伴，该服务器的数据库副本当前是镜像数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2346">The mirror server is the mirroring partner whose copy of the database is currently the mirror database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2347">镜像服务器是热备用服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2347">The mirror server is a hot standby server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2348">镜像介质集 (mirrored media set)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2348">mirrored media set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2349">包含每个介质簇的两个到四个相同副本（镜像）的介质集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2349">A media set that contains two to four identical copies (mirrors) of each media family.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2350">还原操作对于每个介质簇只要求一个镜像，这使已损坏的介质卷能够被镜像中的对应卷替换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2350">Restore operations require only one mirror per family, allowing a damaged media volume to be replaced by the corresponding volume from a mirror.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2351">镜像 (mirroring)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2351">mirroring</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2352">将对读写数据库（主体数据库）所做的每次更新立即重新生成到驻留在单独的数据库引擎实例（镜像服务器）中的该数据库的只读镜像（镜像数据库）中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2352">Immediately reproducing every update to a read-write database (the principal database) onto a read-only mirror of that database (the mirror database) residing on a separate instance of the database engine (the mirror server).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2353">在生产环境中，该镜像服务器位于其他的计算机上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2353">In production environments, the mirror server is on another machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2354">通过还原（但不恢复）主体数据库的完整备份可创建镜像数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2354">The mirror database is created by restoring a full backup of the principal database (without recovery).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2355">model 数据库 (model database)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2355">model database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2356">随 Microsoft SQL Server 一起安装的数据库，为新的用户数据库提供模板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2356">A database that is installed with Microsoft SQL Server and that provides the template for new user databases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2357">SQL Server 通过复制 model 数据库中的内容，然后将新数据库扩展未所需的大小，以创建数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2357">SQL Server creates a database by copying in the contents of the model database and then expanding the new database to the size requested.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2358">模型依赖关系 (model dependency)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2358">model dependency</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2359">两个或更多个模型之间的一种关系，在这种关系中一个模型依赖于其他模型的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2359">A relationship between two or more models in which one model is dependent on the information of another model.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2360">取模 (modulo)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2360">modulo</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2361">其结果为除法运算的余数的算术运算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2361">An arithmetic operation whose result is the remainder of a division operation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2362">例如，7 modulo 3 = 2，这是因为 17 除以 3，余数为 2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2362">For example, 17 modulo 3 = 2 because 17 divided by 3 yields a remainder of 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2363">取模运算在编程中使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2363">Modulo operations are used in programming.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2364">监视服务器 (monitor server)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2364">monitor server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2365">在日志传送配置中，是指配置中的每个日志传送作业记录其历史记录和状态的服务器实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2365">In a log shipping configuration, a server instance on which every log shipping job in the configuration records its history and status.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2366">每个日志传送配置具有自己的专用监视服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2366">Each log shipping configuration has its own dedicated monitor server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2367">msdb</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2367">msdb</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2368">存储计划的作业、警报以及备份/还原历史记录信息的数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2368">A database that stores scheduled jobs, alerts, and backup/restore history information.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2371">多基准差异备份 (multibase differential)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2371">multibase differential</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2372">包含最后一次在非重复基准备份中备份的文件的差异备份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2372">A differential backup that includes files that were last backed up in distinct base backups.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2373">多字节字符集 (multibyte character set)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2373">multibyte character set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2374">混合宽度的字符集，其中某些字符包含 1 个以上的字节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2374">A mixed-width character set, in which some characters consist of more than 1 byte.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2375">MBCS 用于日语、中文和韩语等语言，在这些语言中，256 个单字节字符集的可能值不足以表示所有可能的字符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2375">An MBCS is used in languages such as Japanese, Chinese, and Korean, where the 256 possible values of a single-byte character set are not sufficient to represent all possible characters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2376">多播传递 (multicast delivery)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2376">multicast delivery</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2377">一种通知传递方法，它先对通知设置一次格式，然后将生成的消息发送给多个订阅服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2377">A method for delivering notifications that formats a notification once and sends the resulting message to multiple subscribers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2378">多维表达式 (multidimensional expression)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2378">multidimensional expression</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2379">用来查询和操作多维对象（OLAP 多维数据集）中的数据的语言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2379">A language for querying and manipulating data in multidimensional objects (OLAP cubes).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2380">多维 OLAP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2380">multidimensional OLAP</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2381">一种存储模式，使用专有多维结构存储分区的事实数据和聚合或维度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2381">A storage mode that uses a proprietary multidimensional structure to store a partition's facts and aggregations or a dimension.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2382">多维结构 (multidimensional structure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2382">multidimensional structure</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2383">一种数据库范例，将数据视为单元中包含维度和度量值的多维数据集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2383">A database paradigm that treats data as cubes that contain dimensions and measures in cells.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2390">多用户 (multiuser)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2390">multiuser</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2391">表示可以由多个用户使用的任何计算机系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2391">Pertaining to any computer system that can be used by more than one person.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2392">尽管由多个用户共享的微型计算机可被视为多用户系统，但此术语通常保留用于可由多个用户通过通信工具或通过网络终端同时访问的计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2392">Although a microcomputer shared by several people can be considered a multiuser system, the term is generally reserved for machines that can be accessed simultaneously by several people through communications facilities or via network terminals.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2393">互斥 (mutex)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2393">mutex</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2394">一种编程方法，可确保一次只有一个程序或例程（通常通过使用信号量）能够访问某个资源（如内存分配、I/O 端口或文件）；信号量是在程序用来协调多个程序或例程的活动的标志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2394">A programming technique that ensures that only one program or routine at a time can access some resource, such as a memory location, an I/O port, or a file, often through the use of semaphores, which are flags used in programs to coordinate the activities of more than one program or routine.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2395">我的报表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2395">My Reports</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2396">一个个性化工作区。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2396">A personalized workspace.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2397">我的订阅 (My Subscriptions)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2397">My Subscriptions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2398">列出用户拥有的所有订阅的页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2398">A page that lists all subscriptions that a user owns.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2399">命名缓存 (named cache)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2399">named cache</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2400">内存中存储的可配置单元，具有与其关联的策略，可用于缓存群集中的所有缓存主机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2400">A configurable unit of in-memory storage that has policies associated with it and that is available across all cache hosts in a cache cluster.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2401">命名实例 (named instance)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2401">named instance</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2402">安装并给定了名称的 SQL Server，给定名称是为了与同一台计算机上的其他命名实例和默认实例区分开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2402">An installation of SQL Server that is given a name to differentiate it from other named instances and from the default instance on the same computer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2403">命名管道 (named pipe)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2403">named pipe</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2404">内存的一部分，可被某个进程用来向另一个进程传递信息，因此一个进程的输出就是另一个进程的输入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2404">A portion of memory that can be used by one process to pass information to another process, so that the output of one is the input of the other.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2405">第二个进程可以是本地的（与第一个进程位于同一台计算机上），也可以是远程的（位于联网的计算机上）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2405">The second process can be local (on the same computer as the first) or remote (on a networked computer).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2406">命名更新 (named update)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2406">named update</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2407">一个自定义服务操作，所执行的操作与简单查询、更新、插入或删除操作不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2407">A custom service operation that performs an action which is different than a simple query, update, insert, or delete operation.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2414">本机编译器 (native compiler)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2414">native compiler</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2415">为正在运行它的计算机生成机器码的编译器，与交叉编译器不同，后者为另一种类型的计算机生成代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2415">A compiler that produces machine code for the computer on which it is running, as opposed to a cross-compiler, which produces code for another type of computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2416">大多数编译器为本机编译器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2416">Most compilers are native compilers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2417">本机格式 (native format)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2417">native format</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2418">保持数据库的本机数据类型的本机格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2418">A data format that maintains the native data types of a database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2419">当使用不包含任何扩展/双字节字符集 (DBCS) 字符的数据文件在多个 Microsoft SQL Server 实例之间大容量传输数据时，建议使用本机格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2419">Native format is recommended when you bulk transfer data between multiple instances of Microsoft SQL Server using a data file that does not contain any extended/double-byte character set (DBCS) characters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2420">自然层次结构 (natural hierarchy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2420">natural hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2421">一种层次结构，其中每个级别的成员都与下一个级别的成员之间存在一对多的关系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2421">A hiearchy in which at every level there is a one-to-many relationship between members in that level and members in the next lower level.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2486">对象标识符 (object identifier)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2486">object identifier</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2487">唯一标识对象类或特性的数字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2487">A number that identifies an object class or attribute.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2488">对象标识符 (OID) 在行业范围的全局层次结构中进行组织。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2488">Object identifiers (OIDs) are organized into an industry-wide global hierarchy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2489">对象标识符表示为带点的十进制字符串（如 1.2.3.4），每个圆点表示层次结构中的一个新分支。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2489">An object identifier is represented as a dotted decimal string, such as 1.2.3.4, with each dot representing a new branch in the hierarchy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2490">国家/地区注册机构向个人或组织颁发根对象标识符，后者管理分组在其根对象标识符下的层次结构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2490">National/regional registration authorities issue root object identifiers to individuals or organizations, who manage the hierarchy below their root object identifier.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2491">对象生存期 (object lifetime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2491">object lifetime</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2492">缓存对象位于缓存中且可供缓存客户端检索的时间跨度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2492">The span of time a cached object resides in cache and is available to be retrieved by cache clients.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2493">当对象的生存期结束时，此对象将到期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2493">The object expires when its lifetime ends.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2494">缓存客户端无法检索到期对象，但到期对象保留在缓存主机的内存中，直至被逐出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2494">Expired objects cannot be retrieved by cache clients, but remain in memory of the cache host until they are evicted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2495">指定为生存时间 (TTL)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2495">Specified as time to live (TTL).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2496">对象变量 (object variable)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2496">object variable</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2497">包含对象引用的变量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2497">A variable that contains a reference to an object.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2537">乐观并发</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2537">optimistic concurrency</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2538">一种通过使用缓存对象的版本信息管理并发的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2538">A method of managing concurrency by using a cached object's version information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2539">因为对对象的每个更新都更改其版本号，所以，使用版本信息将阻止更新覆盖其他人的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2539">Because every update to an object changes its version number, using version information prevents the update from overwriting someone else's changes.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2540">优化同步 (optimize synchronization)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2540">optimize synchronization</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2541">合并复制中的选项，允许您在确定最近更改是否导致了某一行移入或移出发布到订阅服务器的分区时尽量降低网络流量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2541">An option in merge replication that allows you to minimize network traffic when determining whether recent changes have caused a row to move into or out of a partition that is published to a Subscriber.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2556">过度拟合 (overfitting)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2556">overfitting</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2557">在数据中的随机变体被错误划分为重要模式类别时数据挖掘中的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2557">A problem in data mining when random variations in data are misclassified as important patterns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2558">在数据集太小以致无法表示真实情况时常常会发生过度拟合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2558">Overfitting often occurs when the data set is too small to represent the real world.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2568">填充 (padding)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2568">padding</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2569">在数据存储中，将一个或多个位（通常是零）添加到数据块以便填充它、将实际数据位强制为某个位置或者禁止数据重复已具有既有含义（例如嵌入命令）的位模式的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2569">In data storage, the addition of one or more bits, usually zeros, to a block of data in order to fill it, to force the actual data bits into a certain position, or to prevent the data from duplicating a bit pattern that has an established meaning, such as an embedded command</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2570">页</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2570">page</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2571">用更小的数据子集返回查询结果，这使用户可通过查看数据“页”来在结果集中导航。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2571">To return the results of a query in smaller subsets of data, thus making it possible for the user to navigate through the result set by viewing 'pages' of data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2572">页</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2572">page</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2573">在虚拟存储系统中，一个固定长度的连续虚拟地址块，在分页操作过程中它作为一个单元在内存和磁盘之间来回复制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2573">In a virtual storage system, a fixed-length block of contiguous virtual addresses copied as a unit from memory to disk and back during paging operations.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2584">PAL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2584">PAL</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2585">用来保护发布服务器的主要机制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2585">The primary mechanism for securing the Publisher.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2586">它包含已获得发布访问权限的登录名、帐户和组的一个列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2586">It contains a list of logins, accounts, and groups that are granted access to the publication.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2587">并行执行 (parallel execution)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2587">parallel execution</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2588">两个或多个例程或程序看似同时发生的执行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2588">The apparently simultaneous execution of two or more routines or programs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2589">并行执行可在单个进程上实现，或者通过使用时间共享技术（例如将程序划分为不同任务或线程的执行）或通过使用多个处理器实现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2589">Concurrent execution can be accomplished on a single process or by using time-sharing techniques, such as dividing programs into different tasks or threads of execution, or by using multiple processors.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2590">并行处理 (parallel processing)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2590">parallel processing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2591">只能在包含两个或多个同时运行的处理器的计算机上运行的处理方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2591">A method of processing that can run only on a computer that contains two or more processors running simultaneously.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2592">在将某一任务分发到可用处理器的方式上，并行处理不同于多处理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2592">Parallel processing differs from multiprocessing in the way a task is distributed over the available processors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2593">在多处理中，一个进程可以划分为多个连续的块，一个处理器管理对数据库的访问，另一个处理器对数据进行分析，第三个处理器处理向屏幕上的图形输出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2593">In multiprocessing, a process might be divided up into sequential blocks, with one processor managing access to a database, another analyzing the data, and a third handling graphical output to the screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2594">使用执行并行处理的系统的程序员必须找到划分任务的方法，以便或多或少在可用处理器之间平均分配任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2594">Programmers working with systems that perform parallel processing must find ways to divide a task so that it is more or less evenly distributed among the processors available.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2595">参数化查询 (parameterized query)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2595">parameterized query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2596">通过参数接受输入值的查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2596">A query that accepts input values through parameters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2597">参数化报表 (parameterized report)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2597">parameterized report</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2598">通过参数接受输入值的发布报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2598">A published report that accepts input values through parameters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2599">参数化行筛选器 (parameterized row filter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2599">parameterized row filter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2600">可以在合并复制中使用的行筛选器，通过它可以基于系统函数或用户定义的函数（例如 SUSER_SNAME()）限制复制到订阅服务器的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2600">A row filter available with merge replication that allows you to restrict the data replicated to a Subscriber based on a system function or user-defined function (for example: SUSER_SNAME()).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2601">部分备份 (partial backup)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2601">partial backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2602">主文件组、每个读-写文件组和任意指定的可选文件中所有数据的备份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2602">A backup of all the data in the primary filegroup, every read-write filegroup, and any optionally specified files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2603">只读数据库的部分备份仅包含主文件组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2603">A partial backup of a read-only database contains only the primary filegroup.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2604">数据库部分还原 (partial database restore)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2604">partial database restore</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2605">只还原数据库的一部分，包括它的主文件组，可能还包括一个或多个辅助文件组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2605">A restore of only a portion of a database consisting of its primary filegroup and one or more secondary filegroups.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2606">其他文件组保持永久脱机，尽管可以在以后还原它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2606">The other filegroups remain permanently offline, though they can be restored later.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2607">部分差异备份 (partial differential backup)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2607">partial differential backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2608">相对于上一次部分备份（基准备份）有差异的部分备份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2608">A partial backup that is differential relative to a single, previous partial backup (the base backup).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2609">对于只读数据库，部分差异备份仅包含主文件组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2609">For a read-only database, a partial differential backup contains only the primary filegroup.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2612">小品词</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2612">particle</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2613">非常小的部分；不可分的对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2613">A very small piece or part; an indivisible object.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2614">分区函数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2614">partition function</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2615">一种函数，它定义如何根据某些列（称为分区依据列）的值将已分区表或索引的行分布到一组分区中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2615">A  function that defines how the rows of a partitioned table or index are spread across a set of partitions based on the values of certain columns, called partitioning columns.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2616">分区方案 (partition scheme)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2616">partition scheme</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2617">将分区函数的分区映射到一组文件组的数据库对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2617">A database object that maps the partitions of a partition function to a set of filegroups.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2618">已分区索引 (partitioned index)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2618">partitioned index</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2619">按分区方案生成的索引，其数据水平划分为多个单元，这些单元可以分布到数据库中的多个文件组中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2619">An index built on a partition scheme, and whose data is horizontally divided into units which may be spread across more than one filegroup in a database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2620">分区快照 (partitioned snapshot)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2620">partitioned snapshot</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2621">在合并复制中，仅包含单个分区中的数据的快照。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2621">In merge replication, a snapshot that includes only the data from a single partition.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2622">已分区表 (partitioned table)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2622">partitioned table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2623">按分区方案生成的表，其数据水平划分为多个单元，这些单元可以分布到数据库中的多个文件组中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2623">A table built on a partition scheme, and whose data is horizontally divided into units which may be spread across more than one filegroup in a database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2624">分区表并行度 (partitioned table parallelism)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2624">partitioned table parallelism</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2625">针对从已分区对象选择的查询的并行执行策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2625">The parallel execution strategy for queries that select from partitioned objects.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2626">作为执行策略的一部分，查询处理器会确定查询所需的表分区，以及要分配给每个分区的线程比例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2626">As part of the execution strategy, the query processor determines the table partitions that are required for the query and the proportion of threads to allocate to each partition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2627">在大多数情况下，查询处理器会为每个分区分配数量相等或几乎相等的线程，然后在这些分区中并行地执行查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2627">In most cases, the query processor allocates an equal or almost equal number of threads to each partition, and then executes the query in parallel across the partitions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2628">partitioning</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2628">partitioning</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2629">使用多个较小的表替换某个表的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2629">The process of replacing a table with multiple smaller tables.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2630">分区依据列 (partitioning column)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2630">partitioning column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2631">分区函数对表或索引进行分区时所使用的表或索引列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2631">The column of a table or index that a partition function uses to partition a table or index.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2632">伙伴 (partner)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2632">partner</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2633">数据库镜像中的主体服务器或镜像服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2633">In database mirroring, refers to the principal server or the mirror server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2634">传递顺序 (pass order)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2634">pass order</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2635">针对多维数据集中的计算成员、自定义成员、自定义汇总公式和计算单元的评估（从最高到最低的计算传递数）和计算顺序（从最低到最高的计算传递数）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2635">The order of evaluation (from highest to lowest calculation pass number) and calculation (from lowest to highest calculation pass number) for calculated members, custom members, custom rollup formulas, and calculated cells in a multidimensional cube.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2636">通行短语 (pass phrase)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2636">pass phrase</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2637">用于获取对网络、程序或数据的访问权限的单词或其他文本的序列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2637">A sequence of words or other text used to gain access to a network, program, or data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2638">通常，通行短语越长，安全性就越高。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2638">A passphrase is generally longer for added security.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2652">对等复制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2652">peer-to-peer replication</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2653">一种事务复制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2653">A type of transactional replication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2654">与只读事务复制和具有更新订阅的事务复制相反，对等复制拓扑中节点之间的关系是对等关系而不是层级关系，每个节点均包含完全相同的架构和数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2654">In contrast to read-only transactional replication and transactional replication with updating subscriptions, the relationships between nodes in a Peer to Peer replication topology are peer relationships rather than hierarchical ones, with each node containing identical schema and data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2655">性能工具 (performance tools)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2655">performance tools</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2656">可用于评估解决方案的性能的工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2656">Tools that you can use to evaluate the performance of a solution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2657">性能工具可具有不同的用途；某些工具设计为评估端到端性能，其他一些工具则着重于评估解决方案的某一特定方面的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2657">Performance tools can have different purposes; some are designed to evaluate end-to-end performance while others focus on evaluating performance of a particular aspect of a solution.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2658">持久化计算列 (persisted computed column)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2658">persisted computed column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2659">物理存储的表的计算列，计算中涉及的任何其他列更改时，其值即更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2659">A computed column of a table that is physically stored, and whose values are updated when any other columns that are part of its computation change.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2660">在某一计算列是确定性的、但不精确时，将持久化属性应用于该列将允许对其创建索引。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2660">Applying the persisted property to a computed column allows for indexes to be created on it when the column is deterministic, but not precise.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2661">持久性数据库 (persistence database)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2661">persistence database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2662">一种持久性存储区，它存储 SQL Server 数据库中的工作流实例状态和工作流实例元数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2662">A type of persistence store that stores workflow instance state and workflow instance metadata in a SQL Server database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2663">透视 (perspective)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2663">perspective</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2664">多维数据集的用户定义的子集，而视图是表的用户定义的子集和关系数据库中的列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2664">A user-defined subset of a cube, whereas a view is a user-defined subset of tables and columns in a relational database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2665">悲观并发</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2665">pessimistic concurrency</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2666">一种管理并发的方法，它通过使用锁技术来阻止其他客户端同时更新相同的对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2666">A method of managing concurrency by using a lock technique to prevent other clients from updating the same object at the same time.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2742">轮询</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2742">polling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2743">定期确定一组设备中每个设备的状态的过程，以便活动程序可以处理每个设备生成的事件，例如是否按下了某一鼠标按钮或者新数据是否是在某一串行端口上提供的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2743">The process of periodically determining the status of each device in a set so that the active program can process the events generated by each device, such as whether a mouse button was pressed or whether new data is available at a serial port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2744">这可能与事件驱动的处理相反，在后者中，操作系统通过中断或消息（而不是不得不依次检查各设备），针对发生的事件对程序或例程发出提醒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2744">This can be contrasted with event-driven processing, in which the operating system alerts a program or routine to the occurrence of an event by means of an interrupt or message rather than having to check each device in turn.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2821">配置文件模板 (profile template)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2821">profile template</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2822">所有 Certificate Lifecycle Manager (CLM) 管理活动的核心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2822">The core of all Certificate Lifecycle Manager (CLM) management activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2823">配置文件模板提供单个管理单元，其中包括管理用户社区在证书的整个生命周期中可能需要的多个证书所需的所有信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2823">The profile template provides a single administrative unit that includes all information necessary to manage the multiple certificates that might be required by a user community throughout the certificate's lifecycle.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2824">配置文件模板还包含与这些证书的最终位置有关的信息，证书可以是基于软件的（即，存储于本地计算机上）或基于硬件的（存储于智能卡上）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2824">A profile template also includes information regarding the final location of those certificates, which can be software-based (that is, stored on the local computer) or hardware-based (stored on a smart card).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2825">配置文件模板不能既包含基于软件的证书，又包含基于智能卡的证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2825">A profile template cannot include both software-based and smart card-based certificates.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2931">RAD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2931">RAD</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2932">一种构建计算机系统的方法，其中，系统按段进行编程和实施，而不是等到完成整个项目后进行实施。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2932">A method of building computer systems in which the system is programmed and implemented in segments, rather than waiting until the entire project is completed for implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2933">由编程人员 James Martin 开发，RAD 使用如 CASE 和 Visual 编程等工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2933">Developed by programmer James Martin, RAD uses such tools as CASE and visual programming.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2934">不齐整层次结构 (ragged hierarchy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2934">ragged hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2935">一种层次结构，其中一个或多个分支中的一个或多个级别不包含成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2935">A hierarchy in which one or more levels do not contain members in one or more branches of the hierarchy.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2936">range</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2936">range</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2937">应用同一时钟向量的一组连续的项标识符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2937">A set of continuous item identifiers to which the same clock vector applies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2938">范围用起点、终点以及应用于起点和终点之间的所有 ID 的时钟向量表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2938">A range is represented by a starting point, an ending point, and a clock vector that applies to all IDs that are in between.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2939">范围分区 (range partition)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2939">range partition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2940">由数据的特定且可自定义的范围定义的一种表分区。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2940">A table partition that is defined by specific and customizable ranges of data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2941">按范围分区 (range partitioning)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2941">range partitioning</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2942">对表或索引进行分区的方法，它通过指定分区来保存单个分区依据列中值在一定范围内的行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2942">A way of partitioning a table or index by specifying partitions to hold rows with ranges of values from a single partitioning column.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2943">范围查询 (range query)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2943">range query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2944">指定值的范围（例如，从 10 到 100 的所有行）作为搜索条件的一部分的查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2944">A query that specifies a range of values as part of the search criteria, such as all rows from 10 through 100.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2945">排名函数 (ranking function)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2945">ranking function</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2946">根据每一行在结果集的窗口（分区）中的位置返回有关该行在窗口中的排名信息的函数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2946">Function that returns ranking information about each row in the window (partition) of a result set depending on the row's position within the window.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2947">快速应用程序开发 (rapid application development)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2947">rapid application development</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2948">一种构建计算机系统的方法，其中，系统按段进行编程和实施，而不是等到完成整个项目后进行实施。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2948">A method of building computer systems in which the system is programmed and implemented in segments, rather than waiting until the entire project is completed for implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2949">由编程人员 James Martin 开发，RAD 使用如 CASE 和 Visual 编程等工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2949">Developed by programmer James Martin, RAD uses such tools as CASE and visual programming.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2950">变动率 (rate of change)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2950">rate of change</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2951">相比于历史记录数据的价格变动率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2951">The rate of price change compared with historical data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2952">变动率是针对当前价格之前的一段日期进行计算的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2952">The rate of change is calculated against a period of days prior to the current price.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2953">输出为百分比值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2953">The output is a percentage.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2954">原始目标适配器 (raw destination adapter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2954">raw destination adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2955">将原始数据写入文件的 SSIS 目标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2955">An SSIS destination that writes raw data to a file.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2964">RDA</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2964">RDA</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2965">一种服务，它为智能设备应用程序访问（请求）远程 SQL Server 数据库表和本地 SQL Server Mobile Edition 数据库表，以及向/从这些数据库表中发送（推送）数据提供了一种简单的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2965">A service that provides a simple way for a smart device application to access (pull) and send (push) data to and from a remote SQL Server database table and a local SQL Server Mobile Edition database table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2966">还可以使用 RDA 在运行 SQL Server 的服务器上发出 SQL 命令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2966">RDA can also be used to issue SQL commands on a server running SQL Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2967">RDBMS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2967">RDBMS</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2968">按关系模型指定的方式将数据组织为相关行和列的数据库系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2968">A database system that organizes data into related rows and columns as specified by a relational model.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2969">RDL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2969">RDL</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2970">描述报表的布局和查询信息的一组指令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2970">A set of instructions that describe layout and query information for a report.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2971">RDL 由 XML 元素组成，这些元素符合为 Reporting Services 创建的 XML 语法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2971">RDL is composed of XML elements that conform to an XML grammar created for Reporting Services.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2972">RDL 沙盒处理 (RDL Sandboxing)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2972">RDL Sandboxing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2973">通过这一功能，您可以在多个租户共享报表服务器的单个 Web 场的情况下检测到和限制单个用户使用的特定类型的资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2973">A feature that makes it possible to detect and restrict specific types of resource use by individual tenants in a scenario where multiple tenants share a single Web farm of report servers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2974">记录集 (record set)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2974">record set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2975">由一组数据库记录组成的数据结构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2975">A data structure made up of a group of database records.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2976">它可以从基表中生成，也可以从对表执行的查询中生成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2976">It can originate from a base table or from a query to the table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2977">recover</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2977">recover</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2978">重新回到一种稳定的情况下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2978">To put back into a stable condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2979">计算机用户可以使用程序搜索和挽回存储设备中保留的任何信息，以恢复丢失或损坏的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2979">A computer user may be able to recover lost or damaged data by using a program to search for and salvage whatever information remains in storage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2980">当出现的问题（如数据库管理程序异常终止）损坏数据库的完整性后，可以通过还原其完整性来恢复数据库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2980">A database may be recovered by restoring its integrity after some problem has damaged it, such as abnormal termination of the database management program.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2981">recovery</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2981">recovery</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2982">使数据库进入事务一致状态的数据库启动阶段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2982">A phase of database startup that brings the database into a transaction-consistent state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2983">恢复可能包括前滚日志记录中的所有事务（重做阶段）和回滚未提交的事务（撤消阶段），具体取决于关闭数据库的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2983">Recovery can include rolling forward all the transactions in the log records (the redo phase) and rolling back uncommitted transactions (the undo phase), depending on how the database was shut down.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2984">恢复分支 (recovery branch)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2984">recovery branch</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2985">共享同一个恢复分支 GUID 的一组 LSN。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2985">A range of LSNs that share the same recovery branch GUID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2986">创建数据库或用 RESTORE WITH RECOVERY 生成恢复分叉之后，会生成新的恢复分支。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2986">A new recovery branch originates when a database is created or when RESTORE WITH RECOVERY generates a recovery fork.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2987">此时可能出现多分支恢复路径，其中包括涵盖两个或多个恢复分叉点的 LSN 范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2987">A multiple-branch recovery path is possible that includes ranges of LSNs that cover two or more recovery fork points.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2988">恢复分叉点 (recovery fork point)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2988">recovery fork point</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2989">每次执行 RESTORE WITH RECOVERY 操作时开始一个新的恢复分支的点 (LSN,GUID)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2989">The point (LSN,GUID) at which a new recovery branch is started, every time a RESTORE WITH RECOVERY is performed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2990">每个恢复分叉都确定了恢复分支之间的父子关系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2990">Each recovery fork determines a parent-child relationship between the recovery branches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2991">如果将数据库恢复到更早的时间点并从该点开始使用数据库，则恢复分叉点会开始一个新的恢复路径。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2991">If you recover a database to an earlier point in time and begin using the database from that point, the recovery fork point starts a new recovery path.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2992">恢复间隔</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2992">recovery interval</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2993">数据库引擎恢复数据库所需的最长时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2993">The maximum amount of time that the Database Engine should require to recover a database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2994">恢复模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2994">recovery model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2995">控制数据库备份和还原操作基本行为的数据库属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2995">A database property that controls the basic behavior of backup and restore operations for a database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2996">例如，恢复模式控制如何记录事务，事务日志是否需要备份，以及可以使用哪些类型的还原操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2996">For instance, the recovery model controls how transactions are logged, whether the transaction log requires backing up, and what kinds of restore operations are available.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2997">恢复路径 (recovery path)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2997">recovery path</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2998">使数据库到达特定时间点（称为恢复点）的一组数据和日志备份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2998">The sequence of data and log backups that have brought a database to a particular point in time (known as a recovery point).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-2999">恢复路径是一组特定的转换，这些转换随着时间的变化对数据库进行演变并保持数据库的一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-2999">A recovery path is a specific set of transformations that have evolved the database over time, yet have maintained the consistency of the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3000">恢复路径描述从“起点”(LSN,GUID) 到“终点”(LSN,GUID) 的一组 LSN。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3000">A recovery path describes a range of LSNs from a start point (LSN,GUID) to an end point (LSN,GUID).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3001">恢复路径中的 LSN 可以从起点到终点遍历一个或多个恢复分支。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3001">The range of LSNs in a recovery path can traverse one or more recovery branches from start to end.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3002">恢复点 (recovery point)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3002">recovery point</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3003">日志链中的点，恢复过程中前滚在该点停止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3003">The point in the log chain at which rolling forward stops during a recovery.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3004">矩形 (rectangle)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3004">rectangle</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3005">一个报表项，可用作多个报表项的容器，也可用作报表上的一个图形元素。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3005">A report item that can be used as a container for multiple report items or as a graphical element on a report.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3006">递归层次结构 (recursive hierarchy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3006">recursive hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3007">所有父子关系都以数据形式表示的数据层次结构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3007">A hierarchy of data in which all parent-child relationships are represented in the data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3008">递归分区 (recursive partitioning)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3008">recursive partitioning</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3009">数据挖掘算法提供程序用来将数据划分为组直至找不到更多有用组的迭代过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3009">The iterative process, used by data mining algorithm providers, of dividing data into groups until no more useful groups can be found.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3010">重做 (redo)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3010">redo</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3011">恢复过程中的一个阶段，通过将记录的更改应用于数据库（前滚），使数据在时间上向前移动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3011">The phase during recovery that applies (rolls forward) logged changes to a database to bring the data forward in time.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3012">重做阶段 (redo phase)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3012">redo phase</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3013">恢复过程中的一个阶段，通过将记录的更改应用于数据库（前滚），使数据在时间上向前移动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3013">The phase during recovery that applies (rolls forward) logged changes to a database to bring the data forward in time.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3014">重做集 (redo set)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3014">redo set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3015">所还原的所有文件和页面的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3015">The set of all files and pages being restored.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3016">引用数据 (reference data)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3016">reference data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3017">特性为共享读取操作且不频繁地发生变化的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3017">Data characterized by shared read operations and infrequent changes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3018">引用数据的示例包括航班计划表和产品目录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3018">Examples of reference data include flight schedules and product catalogs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3019">Windows Server AppFabric 提供了本地缓存功能来存储此类数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3019">Windows Server AppFabric offers the local cache feature for storing this type of data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3020">引用维度 (reference dimension)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3020">reference dimension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3021">维度与度量值组之间的关系，在这种关系中，维度通过另一维度与度量值组关联起来。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3021">A relationship between a dimension and a measure group in which the dimension is coupled to the measure group through another dimension.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3024">被引用键 (referenced key)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3024">referenced key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3025">外键引用的主键或唯一键。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3025">A primary key or unique key referenced by a foreign key.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3026">引用键 (referencing key)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3026">referencing key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3027">某一数据库表中来自另一个表（也称作“被引用表”）的键，并且其值匹配该被引用表中的主键 (PK) 或唯一键。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3027">A key in a database table that comes from another table (also know as the "referenced table") and whose values match the primary key (PK) or unique key in the referenced table.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3030">region</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3030">region</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3031">缓存内数据的容器，它将所有缓存对象一起放置于单个缓存主机中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3031">A container of data, within a cache, that co-locates all cached objects on a single cache host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3032">通过缓存区域，可使用称作标记的说明性字符串搜索该缓存区域中所有缓存的对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3032">Cache Regions enable the ability to search all cached objects in the region by using descriptive strings, called tags.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3033">region</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3033">region</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3034">一个文件中按逻辑顺序排列的 128 个叶级页的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3034">A collection of 128 leaf level pages in logical order in a single file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3035">用来标识已分段文件中的区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3035">Used to identify areas of a file that are fragmented.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3093">复制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3093">replication</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3094">将内容和/或配置设置从一个位置（通常为服务器节点）复制到另一个位置的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3094">The process of copying content and/or configuration settings from one location, generally a server node, to another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3095">执行复制是为了确保同步或故障容错。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3095">Replication is done to ensure synchronization or fault tolerance.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3176">resource</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3176">resource</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3177">报表服务器数据库中除报表项、文件夹项和共享数据源项以外的任何项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3177">Any item in a report server database that is not a report, folder, or shared data source item.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3178">资源数据 (resource data)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3178">resource data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3179">一种类型的数据，其特征为共享、同时读入和写入操作中以及供多个事务访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3179">A type of data that is characterized by shared, concurrently read and written into operations, and accessed by many transactions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3180">资源数据的示例包括用户帐户和拍卖项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3180">Examples of resource data include user accounts and auction items.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3181">资源调控器 (resource governor)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3181">resource governor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3182">SQL Server 2008 中的一项新功能，使用户可以通过指定传入请求的资源消耗限制来控制 SQL Server 工作负荷和资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3182">A feature in SQL Server 2008 that enables the user to manage SQL Server workload and resources by specifying limits on resource consumption by incoming requests.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3183">还原</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3183">restore</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3184">一种包括多个阶段的过程，用于将指定备份中的所有数据和日志页复制到指定数据库（数据复制阶段），然后前滚备份中记录的所有事务（重做阶段）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3184">A multi-phase process that copies all the data and log pages from a specified backup to a specified database (the data-copy phase) and rolls forward all the transactions that are logged in the backup (the redo phase).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3185">此时，在默认情况下，还原将回滚任何不完整的事务（撤消阶段），这会完成数据库的恢复并使其可供用户使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3185">At this point, by default, a restore rolls back any incomplete transactions (the undo phase), which completes the recovery of the database and makes it available to users.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3186">还原顺序 (restore sequence)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3186">restore sequence</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3187">包含一个或多个还原命令的顺序，通常用于初始化要还原的数据库、文件和/或页的内容（数据复制阶段），前滚记录的事务（重做阶段）以及回滚未提交的事务（撤销阶段）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3187">A sequence of one or more restore commands that, typically, initializes the contents of the database, files, and/or pages being restored (the data-copy phase), rolls forward logged transactions (the redo phase), and rolls back uncommitted transactions (the undo phase).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3188">结果集 (result set)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3188">result set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3189">通过运行查询或应用筛选器得到的记录集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3189">The set of records that results from running a query or applying a filter.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3291">架构行集 (schema rowset)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3291">schema rowset</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3292">一个专门定义的行集，它返回 SQL Server 实例或 Analysis Services 实例上的对象或功能的元数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3292">A specially defined rowset that returns metadata about objects or functionality on an instance of SQL Server or Analysis Services.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3293">例如，OLE DB 架构行集 DBSCHEMA_COLUMNS 描述表中的列，而 Analysis Services 架构行集 MDSCHEMA_MEASURES 描述多维数据集中的度量值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3293">For example, the OLE DB schema rowset DBSCHEMA_COLUMNS describes columns in a table, while the Analysis Services schema rowset MDSCHEMA_MEASURES describes the measures in a cube.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3294">架构快照 (schema snapshot)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3294">schema snapshot</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3295">一种快照，其中包括复制所需的已发布表和对象（触发器、元数据表等）的架构，但不包括用户数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3295">A snapshot that includes schema for published tables and objects required by replication (triggers, metadata tables, and so on), but not user data.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3336">安全 ID (security ID)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3336">security ID</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3337">在基于 Windows 的系统中，表示企业内的用户、组或计算机帐户的唯一值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3337">In Windows-based systems, a unique value that identifies a user, group, or computer account within an enterprise.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3338">创建每个帐户时，都会为其颁发一个 SID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3338">Every account is issued a SID when it is created.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3344">自联接 (self-join)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3344">self-join</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3345">将某个表中的记录与同一表中的其他记录相结合（如果联接字段中具有匹配的值）的一种联接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3345">A join in which records from a table are combined with other records from the same table when there are matching values in the joined fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3346">自联接可以是内部联接或外部联接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3346">A self-join can be an inner join or an outer join.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3347">在数据库关系图中，自联接称为反身关系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3347">In database diagrams, a self-join is called a reflexive relationship.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3458">SKU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3458">SKU</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3459">产品的唯一标识符（通常为字母）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3459">A unique identifier, usually alphanumeric, for a product.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3460">通过 SKU 可以跟踪产品来维护库存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3460">The SKU allows a product to be tracked for inventory purposes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3461">SKU 可以与可采购的任何物料关联。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3461">An SKU can be associated with any item that can be purchased.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3462">例如，样式编号为 3726 和尺码为 8 的衬衣的 SKU 可能为 3726-8。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3462">For example, a shirt in style number 3726, size 8 might have a SKU of 3726-8.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3463">sleep</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3463">sleep</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3464">暂停操作但不终止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3464">To suspend operation without terminating.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3465">切片</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3465">slice</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3466">多维数据集中的一个数据子集，通过用维度成员限制一个或多个维度来指定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3466">A subset of the data in a cube, specified by limiting one or more dimensions by members of the dimension.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3467">切片器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3467">Slicers</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3468">提供一次单击筛选控件的一种功能，通过这些控件，可以很轻松地缩小数据集的正查看部分的范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3468">A feature that provides one-click filtering controls that make it easy to narrow down the portion of a data set that's being looked at.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3469">滑动窗口 (sliding window)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3469">sliding window</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3470">固定长度 L 的窗口，该窗口根据流事件沿时间线移动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3470">A window of fixed length L that moves along a timeline according to the stream's events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3471">对于时间线上的每个事件，都会创建一个新窗口，并在事件的开始时间开始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3471">With every event on the timeline, a new window is created, starting at the event's start time.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3472">补充 (slipstream)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3472">slipstream</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3473">将更新、修补程序或 Service Pack 集成到原始软件的基本安装文件中，以便生成的文件允许单步安装更新的软件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3473">To integrate updates, patches or service packs into the base installation files of the original software, so that the resulting files will allow a single step installation of the updated software.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3476">智能卡 (smart card)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3476">smart card</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3477">一个塑料 (信用卡大小或更小) 设备，其中包含一个嵌入的微处理器和少量用于访问代码的存储，用于启用基于证书的身份验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3477">A plastic (credit card-sized or smaller) device with an embedded microprocessor and a small amount of storage that is used, with an access code, to enable certificate-based authentication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3478">智能卡可安全地存储证书、公钥和私钥、密码以及其他类型的个人信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3478">Smart cards securely store certificates, public and private keys, passwords, and other types of personal information.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3496">快照</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3496">snapshot</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3497">一种包含在特定时间点捕获的数据的静态报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3497">A static report that contains data captured at a specific point in time.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3498">快照隔离级别 (snapshot isolation level)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3498">snapshot isolation level</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3499">一种事务隔离级别，其中一个事务执行的每次读取操作都返回该事务开始时存在的所有数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3499">A transaction isolation level in which each read operation performed by a transaction returns all data as it existed at the start of the transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3500">因为快照事务不使用锁来防止读取操作，所以，它不阻止其他事务修改由快照事务读取的任何数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3500">Because a snapshot transaction does not use locks to protect read operations, it will not block other transactions from modifying any data read by the snapshot transaction.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3501">快照复制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3501">snapshot replication</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3502">一种复制方式，其中，数据完全按照其在特定时刻的状态分发，不监视数据是否有更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3502">A replication in which data is distributed exactly as it appears at a specific moment in time and does not monitor for updates to the data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3503">快照共享 (Snapshot Share)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3503">Snapshot Share</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3504">可用于存储快照文件的共享。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3504">A share available for the storage of snapshot files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3505">快照文件包含已发布表的架构和数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3505">Snapshot files contain the schema and data for published tables.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3506">快照窗口 (snapshot window)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3506">snapshot window</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3507">根据流中事件的开始和结束时间（而非时间线上的固定网格）定义的窗口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3507">A window that is defined according to the start and end times of the event in the stream, instead of a fixed grid along the timeline.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3508">雪花型架构 (snowflake schema)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3508">snowflake schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3509">对星型架构的一种扩展，即，由多个表定义一个或多个维度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3509">An extension of a star schema such that one or more dimensions are defined by multiple tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3510">在雪花型架构中，只有主维度表联接到事实数据表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3510">In a snowflake schema, only primary dimension tables are joined to the fact table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3511">其他维度表联接到主维度表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3511">Additional dimension tables are joined to primary dimension tables.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3526">排序顺序 (sort order)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3526">sort order</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3527">一种根据值类型或数据类型对数据进行排列的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3527">A way to arrange data based on value or data type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3528">可以按字母顺序、数字顺序或按日期对数据排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3528">You can sort data alphabetically, numerically, or by date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3529">排序顺序使用升序（1 到 9、A 到 Z）或降序（9 到 1、Z 到 A）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3529">Sort orders use an ascending (1 to 9, A to Z) or descending (9 to 1, Z to A) order.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3538">源代码管理 (source code control)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3538">source code control</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3539">一组功能，其中包括用于检查进出中心存储库的源代码的机制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3539">A set of features that include a mechanism for checking source code in and out of a central repository.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3540">它还指版本控制系统，可以在整个开发生存期中管理文件，同时跟踪发生了哪些更改以及执行更改的用户、时间和原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3540">It also implies a version control system that can manage files through the development lifecycle, keeping track of which changes were made, who made them, when they were made, and why.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3559">稀疏文件 (sparse file)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3559">sparse file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3560">此文件的处理方式需要的磁盘空间要比其他方式少很多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3560">A file that is handled in a way that requires much less disk space than would otherwise be needed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3561">支持稀疏使得应用程序能够创建非常大的文件，而不需要调拨磁盘空间来容纳只包含零的那些文件区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3561">Sparse support allows an application to create very large files without committing disk space for those regions of the file that contain only zeros.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3562">例如，您可以通过稀疏支持来处理 42-GB 文件，其中，您只需向第一个 64 KB 写入数据（文件的剩余部分归零）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3562">For example, you can use sparse support to work with a 42-GB file in which you need to write data only to the first 64 KB (the rest of the file is zeroed).</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3666">SSL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3666">SSL</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3667">一种通过结合使用数据加密、数字证书和公钥密码系统提高数据通信安全性的协议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3667">The protocol that improves the security of data communication by using a combination of data encryption, digital certificates, and public key cryptography.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3668">SSL 支持在网络中进行身份验证并增强数据安全性和隐私。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3668">SSL enables authentication and increases data integrity and privacy over networks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3669">SSL 不提供授权或不可否认性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3669">SSL does not provide authorization or nonrepudiation.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3676">临时数据 (staged data)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3676">staged data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3677">在 SQL Server Master Data Services 的临时过程中导入到临时表中的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3677">Data imported into staging tables during the staging process in SQL Server Master Data Services.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3678">staging</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3678">staging</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3679">SQL Server Master Data Services 中用于将数据导入到临时表中，然后在将临时数据导入到 master 数据库之前将其作为批进行处理的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3679">The process used in SQL Server Master Data Services to import data into staging tables and then process the staged data as a batch prior to importing it into the master database.</span></span>|
