|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3682">临时队列 (staging queue)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3682">staging queue</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3683">SQL Server Master Data Services 中的批处理表，其中，临时记录排队为批处理以等待处理到 Master Data Services 数据库中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3683">The batch table in SQL Server Master Data Services where staged records are queued as batches to be processed into the Master Data Services database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3684">临时表 (staging table)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3684">staging table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3685">SQL Server Master Data Services 中在临时处理过程内用业务数据进行填充的表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3685">A table in SQL Server Master Data Services that is populated with business data during the staging process.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3686">独立服务器 (standalone server)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3686">standalone server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3687">运行 Windows Server 但不参与域的计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3687">A computer that runs Windows Server but does not participate in a domain.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3688">独立服务器只有其自己的最终用户数据库，它自行处理登录请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3688">A standalone server has only its own database of end users, and it processes logon requests by itself.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3689">它不与任何其他计算机共享帐户信息，无法提供对域帐户的访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3689">It does not share account information with any other computer and cannot provide access to domain accounts.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3690">备用文件 (standby file)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3690">standby file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3691">在还原操作中的撤消阶段，用来保存要修改页面的“写入时复制”预映像的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3691">In a restore operation, a file used during the undo phase to hold a "copy-on-write" pre-image of pages that are to be modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3692">通过备用文件可以还原撤消过程，以索回未提交的事务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3692">The standby file allows reverting the undo pass to bring back the uncommitted transactions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3693">备用服务器 (standby server)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3693">standby server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3694">包含数据库副本的服务器实例，如果源数据库不可用，可以使该数据库副本联机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3694">A server instance containing a copy of a database that can be brought online if the source copy of the database becomes unavailable.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3695">日志传送可用于维护“温”备用服务器（称为辅助服务器），其数据库副本定期自动从日志备份中进行更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3695">Log shipping can be used to maintain a "warm" standby server, called a secondary server, whose copy of the database is automatically updated from log backups at regular intervals.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3696">在向温备用服务器执行故障转移之前，必须手动完全更新其数据库副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3696">Before failover to a warm standby server, its copy of the database must be brought fully up to date manually.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3697">可以使用数据库镜像来维护热备用服务器（称为镜像服务器），其数据库副本将持续保持最新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3697">Database mirroring can be used to maintain a "hot" standby server, called a mirror server, whose copy of the database is continuously brought up to date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3698">向镜像服务器上的数据库进行故障转移基本上是瞬间完成的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3698">Failover to the database on a mirror server is essentially instantaneous.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3699">现有查询 (standing query)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3699">standing query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3700">在 StreamInsight 服务器内运行的针对传入事件执行连续计算的查询模板的实例化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3700">An instantiation of a query template that runs within the StreamInsight server performing continuous computation over the incoming events.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3701">星型联接 (star join)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3701">star join</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3702">一个事实数据表（通常为大型事实数据表）与至少两个维度表之间的联接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3702">A join between a fact table (typically a large fact table) and at least two dimension tables.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3703">星型查询 (star query)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3703">star query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3704">将一个事实数据表与多个维度表相联接的查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3704">A query that joins a fact table and a number of dimension tables.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3705">星型架构 (star schema)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3705">star schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3706">一种关系数据库结构，其中数据保存在架构中心的一个事实数据表中，而其他维度数据存储在维度表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3706">A relational database structure in which data is maintained in a single fact table at the center of the schema with additional dimension data stored in dimension tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3707">每个维度表按键列直接与事实数据表相关并通常联接到事实数据表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3707">Each dimension table is directly related to and usually joined to the fact table by a key column.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3708">开始角度 (start angle)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3708">start angle</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3709">介于 0 至 360 之间的旋转角度，是刻度的起始位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3709">The angle of rotation, between 0 and 360, at which the scale will begin.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3710">位置零 (0) 位于仪表的底部，开始角度按顺时针方向旋转。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3710">The zero (0) position is located at the bottom of the gauge, and the start angle rotates clockwise.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3711">例如，如开始角度为 90 度，将使刻度从 9 点钟位置开始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3711">For example, a start angle of 90 degrees starts the scale at the 9 o'clock position.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3712">起始线帽 (start cap)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3712">start cap</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3713">线条的起点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3713">The start of a line.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3714">statement</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3714">statement</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3715">已编译的 T-SQL 查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3715">A compiled T-SQL query.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3718">静态行筛选器 (static row filter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3718">static row filter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3719">一种可用于所有复制类型的筛选器，允许基于 WHERE 子句限制复制到订阅服务器上的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3719">A filter available for all types of replication that allows you to restrict the data replicated to a Subscriber based on a WHERE clause.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3720">stemmer</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3720">stemmer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3721">在全文搜索中，对于某种给定的语言，词干分析器可基于该语言的规则生成某个特定词的变形形式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3721">In Full-Text Search, for a given language, a stemmer generates inflectional forms of a particular word based on the rules of that language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3722">词干分析器特定于语言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3722">Stemmers are language specific.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3723">单步执行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3723">step into</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3724">若要执行当前语句并进入中断模式，只要出现对另一个过程的调用，就会逐语句执行下一个过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3724">To execute the current statement and enter Break mode, stepping into the next procedure whenever a call for another procedure is reached.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3727">单品 (stock keeping unit)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3727">stock keeping unit</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3728">产品的唯一标识符（通常为字母）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3728">A unique identifier, usually alphanumeric, for a product.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3729">通过 SKU 可以跟踪产品来维护库存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3729">The SKU allows a product to be tracked for inventory purposes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3730">SKU 可以与可采购的任何物料关联。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3730">An SKU can be associated with any item that can be purchased.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3731">例如，样式编号为 3726 和尺码为 8 的衬衣的 SKU 可能为 3726-8。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3731">For example, a shirt in style number 3726, size 8 might have a SKU of 3726-8.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3734">非索引字表 (stoplist)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3734">stoplist</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3735">所谓的非索引字的特定集合，非索引字通常频繁出现在文档中但被认为并没有传达有用的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3735">A specific collection of so-called stopwords, which tend to appear frequently in documents, but are believed to carry no usable information.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3736">非索引字 (stopword)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3736">stopword</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3737">通常频繁出现在文档中但并没有传达有用信息的字词。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3737">A word that tends to appear frequently in documents and carries no usable information.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3738">存储引擎 (storage engine)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3738">storage engine</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3739">SQL Server 的一个组件，负责管理数据库中的原始物理数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3739">A component of SQL Server that is responsible for managing the raw physical data in your database.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3740">例如，向磁盘读取数据就是一个由存储引起处理的任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3740">For example, reading and writing the data to disk is a task handled by the storage engine.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3746">存储过程冲突解决程序 (stored procedure resolver)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3746">stored procedure resolver</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3747">所调用的用于处理基于行更改的冲突的程序（这些冲突是在冲突解决程序所注册到的项目中遇到的）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3747">A program that is invoked to handle row change-based conflicts that are encountered in an article to which the resolver was registered.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3748">流 (stream)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3748">stream</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3749">字节序列的抽象，例如文件、I/O 设备、进程中通信管道、TCP/IP 套接字或进行后台处理的打印作业。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3749">An abstraction of a sequence of bytes, such as a file, an I/O device, an inter-process communication pipe, a TCP/IP socket, or a spooled print job.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3750">复合文件中流与存储之间的关系类似于文件与文件夹之间的关系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3750">The relationship between streams and storages in a compound file is similar to that of files and folders.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3970">跟踪令牌 (tracer token)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3970">tracer token</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3971">一种性能监视工具，可用于进行事务复制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3971">A performance monitoring tool available for transactional replication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3972">令牌（少量数据）通过复制系统进行发送，以测量事务到达分发服务器和订阅服务器所需的时间量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3972">A token (a small amount of data) is sent through the replication system to measure the amount of time it takes for transactions to reach the Distributor and Subscribers.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3987">事务日志备份 (transaction log backup)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3987">transaction log backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3988">包括以前日志备份中未备份的所有日志记录的事务日志备份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3988">A backup of transaction logs that includes all log records not backed up in previous log backups.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-3989">在完整恢复模式或大容量日志恢复模式下需要进行日志备份，但在简单恢复模式下不可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-3989">Log backups are required under the full and bulk-logged recovery models and are unavailable under the simple recovery model.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4020">类型检查 (type checking)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4020">type checking</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4021">由编译器或解释器执行的过程，用于确保当使用某个变量时，该变量的数据类型与声明它时的数据类型相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4021">The process performed by a compiler or interpreter to make sure that when a variable is used, it is treated as having the same data type as it was declared to have.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4031">非均衡层次结构 (unbalanced hierarchy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4031">unbalanced hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4032">一种层次结构，其中一个或多个分支中的一个或多个级别不包含成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4032">A hierarchy in which one or more levels do not contain members in one or more branches of the hierarchy.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4033">未绑定流 (unbound stream)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4033">unbound stream</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4034">包含事件模型或负载类型的定义但不定义数据源的事件流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4034">An event stream that contains the definition of the event model or payload type, but does not define the data source.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4035">不可提交的 (uncommittable)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4035">uncommittable</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4036">所涉及的是保持打开状态但无法完成的事务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4036">Pertaining to a transaction that remains open and cannot be completed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4037">无法提交的事务可被视为部分失败的事务的子类，其中事务遇到了阻止其完成的错误，但它仍保留其锁且必须由用户进行回滚。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4037">Uncommitable transactions could be considered a subclass of partially failed transactions, where the transaction has encountered an error that prevents its completion, but it is still holding its locks and has to be rolled back by the user.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4038">解压缩 (uncompress)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4038">uncompress</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4039">将压缩文件的内容还原为其原始格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4039">To restore the contents of a compressed file to its original form.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4040">无法传递 (undeliverable)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4040">undeliverable</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4041">无法传递给目标收件人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4041">Not able to be delivered to an intended recipient.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4042">如果无法传递电子邮件，则电子邮件将返回给发件人，并且邮件服务器将添加说明问题的信息；例如，电子邮件地址可能不正确，或者收件人的邮箱可能已满。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4042">If an e-mail message is undeliverable, it is returned to the sender with information added by the mail server explaining the problem; for example, the e-mail address may be incorrect, or the recipient's mailbox may be full.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4043">基础表 (underlying table)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4043">underlying table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4044">由视图、游标或存储过程引用的表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4044">A table referenced by a view, cursor, or stored procedure.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4045">撤消 (undo)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4045">undo</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4046">数据库恢复过程中的一个阶段，在此阶段，将取消（回滚）在恢复的重做阶段完成时仍未提交的所有事务所做的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4046">The phase during database recovery that reverses (rolls back) changes made by any transactions that were uncommitted when the redo phase of recovery completed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4047">撤消文件 (undo file)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4047">undo file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4048">当未提交的回滚事务修改了数据库中页面的内容后，但在恢复操作将内容还原到其先前状态之前，保存这些内容的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4048">A file that saves the content of the pages in a database after they've been modified by uncommitted, rolled back transactions and before recovery restores them to their previous state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4049">撤消文件可防止丢失由未提交的事务执行的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4049">The undo file prevents the changes performed by uncommitted transactions from being lost.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4050">撤消阶段 (undo phase)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4050">undo phase</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4051">数据库恢复过程中的一个阶段，在此阶段，将取消（回滚）在恢复的重做阶段完成时仍未提交的所有事务所做的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4051">The phase during database recovery that reverses (rolls back) changes made by any transactions that were uncommitted when the redo phase of recovery completed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4052">非强制关系 (unenforced relationship)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4052">unenforced relationship</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4053">表之间的一种联系，将一个表中的主键与另一个表中的外键关联起来，并且在 INSERT 和 UPDATE 事务执行期间不检查引用完整性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4053">A link between tables that references the primary key in one table to a foreign key in another table, and which does not check the referential integrity during INSERT and UPDATE transactions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4054">取消初始化 (uninitialize)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4054">uninitialize</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4055">更改枚举器或数据源对象的状态，以便其无法用于访问数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4055">To change the state of an enumerator or data source object so that it cannot be used to access data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4056">唯一索引 (unique index)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4056">unique index</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4057">一种索引，采用这种索引时各行的索引值必须都不相同，因而可禁止出现索引或键值重复的情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4057">An index in which no two rows are permitted to have the same index value, thus prohibiting duplicate index or key values.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4058">uniqueifier</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4058">uniqueifier</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4059">一个占用 4 个字节的列，由 SQL Server 数据库引擎自动添加到行中，以使每个索引键保持唯一。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4059">A 4-byte column that the SQL Server Database Engine automatically adds to a row to make each index key unique.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4109">版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4109">version</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4110">一个用于区分缓存中存储的使用相同键的对象的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4110">A property that is used to differentiate objects stored in the cache using the same key.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4111">Windows Server AppFabric 使用 DataCacheItemVersion 类存储版本信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4111">Windows Server AppFabric stores the version information using the DataCacheItemVersion class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4112">每次在缓存中添加或更新对象时，版本值都会更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4112">Every time an object is added or updated in the cache, the version value changes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4113">版本控制用于维护数据一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4113">Versioning is used to maintain data consistency.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4114">乐观并发是使用版本控制而非锁来实现的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4114">Optimistic concurrency is achieved by using versioning as opposed to locks.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4128">牺牲品 (victim)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4128">victim</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4129">当 tempdb 用完了空间且数据库引擎强制版本存储区收缩时，尚未生成行版本的运行时间最长的事务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4129">The longest running transaction that has not generated row versions when tempdb runs out of space and the Database Engine forces the version stores to shrink.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4130">在错误日志中为每个作为牺牲品的事务生成消息 3967。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4130">A message 3967 is generated in the error log for each victim transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0d9f-4131">如果某个事务被标记为牺牲品，则该事务不能再读取版本存储区中的行版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0d9f-4131">If a transaction is marked as a victim, it can no longer read the row versions in the version store.</span></span>|
